EU rejects German call to boycott British lamb . 
107000700

Peter Blackburn 
34

BRUSSELS 1996-08-22 
50

The European Commission said on Thursday it disagreed with German advice to consumers to shun British lamb until scientists determine whether mad cow disease can be transmitted to sheep . 
012000000700000700000000000000

Germany 's representative to the European Union 's veterinary committee Werner Zwingmann said on Wednesday consumers should buy sheepmeat from countries other than Britain until the scientific advice was clearer . 
5000012000340000000000050000000

" We do n't support any such recommendation because we do n't see any grounds for it , " the Commission 's chief spokesman Nikolaus van der Pas told a news briefing . 
000000000000000000001000344400000

He said further scientific study was required and if it was found that action was needed it should be taken by the European Union . 
0000000000000000000000120

He said a proposal last month by EU Farm Commissioner Franz Fischler to ban sheep brains , spleens and spinal cords from the human and animal food chains was a highly specific and precautionary move to protect human health . 
0000000100340000000000000000000000000000

Fischler proposed EU-wide measures after reports from Britain and France that under laboratory conditions sheep could contract Bovine Spongiform Encephalopathy ( BSE ) -- mad cow disease . 
3070000505000000078807000000

But Fischler agreed to review his proposal after the EU 's standing veterinary committee , mational animal health officials , questioned if such action was justified as there was only a slight risk to human health . 
0300000001000000000000000000000000000

Spanish Farm Minister Loyola de Palacio had earlier accused Fischler at an EU farm ministers ' meeting of causing unjustified alarm through " dangerous generalisation . " 
700344000300100000000000000

. 
0

Only France and Britain backed Fischler 's proposal . 
050503000

The EU 's scientific veterinary and multidisciplinary committees are due to re-examine the issue early next month and make recommendations to the senior veterinary officials . 
01000000000000000000000000

Sheep have long been known to contract scrapie , a brain-wasting disease similar to BSE which is believed to have been transferred to cattle through feed containing animal waste . 
000000000000007000000000000000

British farmers denied on Thursday there was any danger to human health from their sheep , but expressed concern that German government advice to consumers to avoid British lamb might influence consumers across Europe . 
70000000000000000000700000070000050

" What we have to be extremely careful of is how other countries are going to take Germany 's lead , " Welsh National Farmers ' Union ( NFU ) chairman John Lloyd Jones said on BBC radio . 
000000000000000005000012222010034400120

Bonn has led efforts to protect public health after consumer confidence collapsed in March after a British report suggested humans could contract an illness similar to mad cow disease by eating contaminated beef . 
5000000000000000700000000000000000

Germany imported 47,600 sheep from Britain last year , nearly half of total imports . 
500005000000000

It brought in 4,275 tonnes of British mutton , some 10 percent of overall imports . 
0000007000000000

Rare Hendrix song draft sells for almost $ 17,000 . 
0300000000

LONDON 1996-08-22 
50

A rare early handwritten draft of a song by U.S. guitar legend Jimi Hendrix was sold for almost $ 17,000 on Thursday at an auction of some of the late musician 's favourite possessions . 
00000000050034000000000000000000000

A Florida restaurant paid 10,925 pounds ( $ 16,935 ) for the draft of " Ai n't no telling " , which Hendrix penned on a piece of London hotel stationery in late 1966 . 
05000000000000078880003000005000000

At the end of a January 1967 concert in the English city of Nottingham he threw the sheet of paper into the audience , where it was retrieved by a fan . 
00000000007005000000000000000000

Buyers also snapped up 16 other items that were put up for auction by Hendrix 's former girlfriend Kathy Etchingham , who lived with him from 1966 to 1969 . 
000000000000003000340000000000

They included a black lacquer and mother of pearl inlaid box used by Hendrix to store his drugs , which an anonymous Australian purchaser bought for 5,060 pounds ( $ 7,845 ) . 
000000000000030000000070000000000

The guitarist died of a drugs overdose in 1970 aged 27 .

German July car registrations up 14.2 pct yr / yr . 
70000000000

FRANKFURT 1996-08-22 
50

German first-time registrations of motor vehicles jumped 14.2 percent in July this year from the year-earlier period , the Federal office for motor vehicles said on Thursday . 
7000000000000000000122220000

The office said 356,725 new cars were registered in July 1996 -- 304,850 passenger cars and 15,613 trucks . 
0000000000000000000

The figures represent a 13.6 percent increase for passenger cars and a 2.2 percent decline for trucks from July 1995 . 
000000000000000000000

Motor-bike registration rose 32.7 percent in the period . 
000000000

The growth was partly due to an increased number of Germans buying German cars abroad , while manufacturers said that domestic demand was weak , the federal office said . 
000000000070700000000000000000

Almost all German car manufacturers posted gains in registration numbers in the period . 
00700000000000

Volkswagen AG won 77,719 registrations , slightly more than a quarter of the total . 
120000000000000

Opel AG together with General Motors came in second place with 49,269 registrations , 16.4 percent of the overall figure . 
120012000000000000000

Third was Ford with 35,563 registrations , or 11.7 percent . 
00100000000

Only Seat and Porsche had fewer registrations in July 1996 compared to last year 's July . 
01010000000000000

Seat posted 3,420 registrations compared with 5522 registrations in July a year earlier . 
10000000000000

Porsche 's registrations fell to 554 from 643 . 
100000000

Colleen Siegel 
34

JERUSALEM 1996-08-22 
50

Israel 's outgoing peace negotiator with Syria said on Thursday current tensions between the two countries appeared to be a storm in a teacup . 
5000005000000000000000000

Itamar Rabinovich , who as Israel 's ambassador to Washington conducted unfruitful negotiations with Syria , told Israel Radio it looked like Damascus wanted to talk rather than fight . 
340005000500005001200050000000

" It appears to me the Syrian priority is still to negotiate . 
0000007000000

The Syrians are confused , they are definitely tense , but the general assessment here in Washington is that this is essentially a storm in a teacup , " he said . 
07000000000000005000000000000000

Rabinovich is winding up his term as ambassador . 
300000000

He will be replaced by Eliahu Ben-Elissar , a former Israeli envoy to Egypt and right-wing Likud party politician . 
00000340007005001000

Israel on Wednesday sent Syria a message , via Washington , saying it was committed to peace and wanted to open negotiations without preconditions . 
5000500005000000000000000

But it slammed Damascus for creating what it called a dangerous atmosphere . 
0005000000000

Syria accused Israel on Wednesday of launching a hysterical campaign against it after Israeli television reported that Damascus had recently test fired a missile . 
5050000000000700050000000

It said its arms purchases were for defensive purposes . 
0000000000

" The message that we sent to ( Syrian President Hafez al- ) Assad is that Israel is ready at any time without preconditions to enter peace negotiations , " Israeli Foreign Minister David Levy told Israel Radio in an interview . 
000000007034030050000000000000700340120000

Tension has mounted since Israeli Prime Minister Benjamin Netanyahu took office in June vowing to retain the Golan Heights Israel captured from Syria in the 1967 Middle East war . 
000070034000000005650050005600

Israeli-Syrian peace talks have been deadlocked over the Golan since 1991 despite the previous government 's willingness to make Golan concessions . 
7000000050000000000500

Peace talks between the two sides were last held in February . 
000000000000

" The voices coming out of Damascus are bad , not good . 
0000005000000

The media ... 
000

are full of expressions and declarations that must be worrying ... 
00000000000

this artificial atmosphere is very dangerous because those who spread it could become its prisoners , " Levy said . 
00000000000000000300

" We expect from Syria , if its face is to peace , that it will answer Israel 's message to enter peace negotiations because that is our goal , " he said . " 
00005000000000000500000000000000000

We do not want a war , God forbid . 
0000000300

No one benefits from wars . " 
0000000

Israel 's Channel Two television said Damascus had sent a " calming signal " to Israel . 
50120050000000050

It gave no source for the report . 
00000000

Netanyahu and Levy 's spokesmen said they could not confirm it . 
303000000000

-- Amsterdam newsroom +31 20 504 5000 
0500000

German farm ministry tells consumers to avoid British mutton . 
7000000700

BONN 1996-08-22 
50

Germany 's Agriculture Ministry suggested on Wednesday that consumers avoid eating meat from British sheep until scientists determine whether mad cow disease can be transmitted to the animals . 
50120000000007000000000000000

" Until this is cleared up by the European Union 's scientific panels -- and we have asked this to be done as quickly as possible -- ( consumers ) should if at all possible give preference to sheepmeat from other countries , " ministry official Werner Zwingmann told ZDF television . 
0000000012000000000000000000000000000000000000340100

" I do not want to say that there is a concrete danger for consumers , " he added . " 
000000000000000000000

There are too many holes in what we know , and these must be filled very quickly . " 
0000000000000000000

Bonn has led efforts to ensure consumer protection tops the list of priorities in dealing with the mad cow crisis , which erupted in March when Britain acknowledged humans could contract a similar illness by eating contaminated beef . 
500000000000000000000000005000000000000

The European Commission agreed this month to rethink a proposal to ban the use of suspect sheep tissue after some EU veterinary experts questioned whether it was justified . 
01200000000000000000100000000

EU Farm Commissioner Franz Fischler had proposed banning sheep brains , spleens and spinal cords from the human and animal food chains after reports from Britain and France that under laboratory conditions sheep could contract Bovine Spongiform Encephalopathy ( BSE ) -- mad cow disease . 
1003400000000000000000000505000000078807000000

But some members of the EU 's standing veterinary committee questioned whether the action was necessary given the slight risk to human health . 
000001000000000000000000

The question is being studied separately by two EU scientific committees . 
000000001000

Sheep have long been known to contract scrapie , a similar brain-wasting disease to BSE which is believed to have been transferred to cattle through feed containing animal waste . 
000000000000007000000000000000

British officials say sheep meat is perfectly safe to eat . 
70000000000

ZDF said Germany imported 47,600 sheep from Britain last year , nearly half of total imports . 
10500005000000000

It brought in 4,275 tonnes of British mutton , some 10 percent of overall imports . 
0000007000000000

After the British government admitted a possible link between mad cow disease and its fatal human equivalent , the EU imposed a worldwide ban on British beef exports . 
00700000000000000001000007000

EU leaders agreed at a summit in June to a progressive lifting of the ban as Britain takes parallel measures to eradicate the disease . 
1000000000000000500000000

HORSE RACING - PIVOTAL ENDS 25-YEAR WAIT FOR TRAINER PRESCOTT . 
00030000030

YORK , England 1996-08-22 
5050

Sir Mark Prescott landed his first group one victory in 25 years as a trainer when his top sprinter Pivotal , a 100-30 chance , won the Nunthorpe Stakes on Thursday . 
03400000000000000003000000078000

The three-year-old , partnered by veteran George Duffield , snatched a short head verdict in the last stride to deny Eveningperformance ( 16-1 ) , trained by Henry Candy and ridden by Chris Rutter . 
00000034000000000000300000034000340

Hever Golf Rose ( 11-4 ) , last year 's Prix de l ' Abbaye winner at Longchamp , finished third , a further one and a quarter lengths away with the 7-4 favourite Mind Games in fourth . 
344000000078888005000000000000000034000

Pivotal , a Royal Ascot winner in June , may now be aimed at this season 's Abbaye , Europe 's top sprint race . 
3003400000000000070500000

Prescott , reluctant to go into the winner 's enclosure until the result of the photo-finish was announced , said : " Twenty-five years and I have never been there so I thought I had better wait a bit longer . " 
300000000000000000000000000000000000000000

He added : " It 's very sad to beat Henry Candy because I am godfather to his daughter . " 
000000000034000000000

Like Prescott , Jack Berry , trainer of Mind Games , had gone into Thursday 's race in search of a first group one success after many years around the top of his profession . 
03034000340000000000000000000000000

Berry said : " I`m disappointed but I do n't feel suicidal . 
3000000000000

He ( Mind Games ) was going as well as any of them one and a half furlongs ( 300 metres ) out but he just did n't quicken . "

TENNIS - NEWCOMBE PONDERS HIS DAVIS CUP FUTURE . 
003007800

SYDNEY 1996-08-22 
50

Australian Davis Cup captain John Newcombe on Thursday signalled his possible resignation if his team loses an away tie against Croatia next month . 
778034000000000000005000

The former Wimbledon champion said the immediate future of Australia 's Davis Cup coach Tony Roche could also be determined by events in Split . 
0070000005078034000000050

" If we lose this one , Tony and I will have to have a good look at giving someone else a go , " Newcombe was quoted as saying in Sydney 's Daily Telegraph newspaper . 
0000000300000000000000000300000501200

Australia face Croatia in the world group qualifying tie on clay from September 20-22 . 
505000000000000

Under Newcombe 's leadership , Australia were relegated from the elite world group last year , the first time the 26-time Davis Cup winners had slipped from the top rank . 
0300050000000000000007800000000

Since taking over as captain from Neale Fraser in 1994 , Newcombe 's record in tandem with Roche , his former doubles partner , has been three wins and three losses . 
00000034000300000300000000000000

Newcombe has selected Wimbledon semifinalist Jason Stoltenberg , Patrick Rafter , Mark Philippoussis , and Olympic doubles champions Todd Woodbridge and Mark Woodforde to face the Croatians . 
3007034034034007003403400070

The home side boasts world number six Goran Ivanisevic , and Newcombe conceded his players would be hard-pressed to beat the Croatian number one . 
0000000340030000000007000

" We are ready to fight to our last breath -- Australia must play at its absolute best to win , " said Newcombe , who described the tie as the toughest he has faced as captain . 
00000000000500000000000300000000000000

Australia last won the Davis Cup in 1986 , but they were beaten finalists against Germany three years ago under Fraser 's guidance . 
500078000000000500003000

BASEBALL - ORIOLES ' MANAGER DAVEY JOHNSON HOSPITALIZED . 
001003400

BALTIMORE 1996-08-22 
50

Baltimore Orioles manager Davey Johnson will miss Thursday night 's game against the Seattle Mariners after being admitted to a hospital with an irregular heartbeat . 
12034000000001200000000000

The 53-year-old Johnson was hospitalized after experiencing dizziness . 
003000000

" He is in no danger and will be treated and observed this evening , " said Orioles team physician Dr. William Goldiner , adding that Johnson is expected to be released on Friday . 
00000000000000000100034000300000000

Orioles ' bench coach Andy Etchebarren will manage the club in Johnson 's absence . 
100034000003000

Johnson is the second manager to be hospitalized this week after California Angels skipper John McNamara was admitted to New York 's Columbia Presbyterian Hospital on Wednesday with a blood clot in his left calf . 
300000000001203400056056600000000000

Johnson , who played eight seasons in Baltimore , was named Orioles manager in the off-season replacing Phil Regan . 
30000005000100000340

He led the Cincinnati Reds to the National League Championship Series last year and guided the New York Mets to a World Series championship in 1986 . 
000120078880000012200780000

Baltimore has won 16 of its last 22 games to pull within five games of the slumping New York Yankees in the American League East Division . 
100000000000000001220078880

BASEBALL - GREER HOMER IN 10TH LIFTS TEXAS PAST INDIANS . 
00300001010

CLEVELAND 1996-08-22 
50

Rusty Greer 's two-run homer in the top of the 10th inning rallied the Texas Rangers to a 10-8 victory over the Cleveland Indians Wednesday in the rubber game of a three-game series between division leaders . 
3400000000000012000000120000000000000

With one out , Greer hit a 1-1 pitch from Julian Tavarez ( 4-7 ) over the right-field fence for his 15th home run . 
0000300000340000000000000

" It was an off-speed pitch and I just tried to get a good swing on it and put it in play , " Greer said . " 
0000000000000000000000003000

This was a big game . 
000000

The crowd was behind him and it was intense . " 
00000000000

The shot brought home Ivan Rodriguez , who had his second double of the game , giving him 42 this season , 41 as a catcher . 
000034000000000000000000000

He joined Mickey Cochrane , Johnny Bench and Terry Kennedy as the only catchers with 40 doubles in a season . 
003403403400000000000

The Rangers have won 10 of their last 12 games and six of nine meetings against the Indians this season . 
010000000000000001000

The American League Western leaders have won eight of 15 games at Jacobs Field , joining the Yankees as the only teams with a winning record at the A.L. Central leaders ' home . 
0788000000005600010000000000780000

Cleveland lost for just the second time in six games . 
10000000000

The Indians sent the game into extra innings in the ninth on Kenny Lofton 's two-run single . 
010000000000340000

Ed Vosberg ( 1-0 ) blew his first save opportunity but got the win , allowing three hits with two walks and three strikeouts in 1 2/3 scoreless innings . 
340000000000000000000000000000

Dean Palmer hit his 30th homer for the Rangers . 
3400000010

In Baltimore , Cal Ripken had four hits and snapped a fifth-inning tie with a solo homer and Bobby Bonilla added a three-run shot in the seventh to power the surging Orioles to a 10-5 victory over the Seattle Mariners . 
05034000000000000034000000000001000000120

The Mariners scored four runs in the top of the fifth to tie the game 5-5 but Ripken led off the bottom of the inning with his 21st homer off starter Sterling Hitchcock ( 12-6 ) . 
0100000000000000030000000000000340000

Bonilla 's blast was the first time Randy Johnson , last season 's Cy Young winner , allowed a run in five relief appearances since coming off the disabled list on August 6 . 
3000000340000340000000000000000000

Bonilla has 21 RBI and 15 runs in his last 20 games . 
3007000000000

Baltimore has won seven of nine and 16 of its last 22 and cut the Yankees ' lead in the A.L. East to five games . 
50000000000000010000780000

Scott Erickson ( 8-10 ) laboured to his third straight win . 
340000000000

340000070010000000000000

He became the fifth shortstop in major-league history to hit 30 homers in a season and the first since Ripken hit 34 in 1991 . 
0000000000000000000300000

Chris Hoiles hit his 22nd homer for Baltimore . 
340000050

05603400000000000034000000000001200100

3000034000000000

05034000000000001200000000120

CRICKET - POLICE COMMANDOS ON HAND FOR AUSTRALIANS ' FIRST MATCH . 
000000070000

COLOMBO 1996-08-22 
50

Armed police commandos patrolled the ground when Australia opened their short tour of Sri Lanka with a five-run win over the country 's youth team on Thursday . 
0000000500000560000000000000

Australia , in Sri Lanka for a limited overs tournament which also includes India and Zimbabwe , have been promised the presence of commandos , sniffer dogs and plainclothes policemen to ensure the tournament is trouble-free . 
5005600000000505000000000000000000000

They are making their first visit to the island since boycotting a World Cup fixture in February because of fears over ethnic violence . 
000000000000780000000000

Australia , batting first in Thursday 's the warm-up match , scored 251 for seven from their 50 overs . 
50000000000000000000

Ricky Ponting led the way with 100 off 119 balls with two sixes and nine fours before retiring . 
3400000000000000000

The youth side replied with 246 for seven . 
000000000

Australian coach Geoff Marsh said he was impressed with the competitiveness of the opposition . 
703400000000000

" We were made to sweat to win , " he said . 
0000000000000

Measles exposure can lead to bowel disease - study . 
0000000000

LONDON 1996-08-23 
50

Women who get measles while pregnant may have babies at higher risk of Crohn 's disease , a debilitating bowel disorder , researchers said on Friday . 
000000000000030000000000000

Three out of four Swedish babies born to mothers who caught measles developed serious cases of Crohn 's disease , the researchers said . 
000070000000000030000000

Dr Andrew Wakefield of the Royal Free Hospital School of Medicine and colleagues screened 25,000 babies delivered at University Hospital , Uppsala , between 1940 and 1949 . 
0340056666600000005605000000

Four of the mothers had measles while pregnant . 
000000000

" Three of the four children had Crohn 's disease , " Wakefield 's group wrote in the Lancet medical journal . 
0000000300003000001000

Crohn 's is an inflammation of the bowel that can sometimes require surgery . 
30000000000000

It causes diarrhoea , abdominal pain and weight loss . 
0000000000

The researchers said the three children involved had especially severe cases . 
000000000000

Exposure to viruses can often cause birth defects . 
000000000

Most notably , women who get rubella ( German measles ) have a high risk of a stillborn baby .

Garlic pills do n't lower cholesterol , study finds . 
0000000000

LONDON 1996-08-22 
50

Garlic pills may not lower blood cholesterol and studies that show they do may be flawed , British researchers have reported . 
0000000000000000070000

A study by a team of doctors at Oxford University has found people with high blood cholesterol do not benefit significantly from taking garlic tablets . 
00000000120000000000000000

The study involved 115 people with high blood cholesterol levels . 
00000000000

They were given 900 milligrams a day of dried garlic powder or placebo tablets . " 
0000000000000000

There were no significant differences between the groups receiving garlic and placebo , " they wrote in the Journal of the Royal College of Physicians . 
00000000000000000012222220

Those taking part were told to eat a low-fat diet for six weeks before they started taking the pills , and their blood cholesterol measured before and after the six-week period . 
00000000000000000000000000000000

The researchers said this would make their findings more accurate . 
00000000000

Several studies have found garlic pills can lower blood pressure and blood cholesterol . 
00000000000000

But the Oxford team disputed these findings and said either previous trials may have been interpreted incorrectly , those taking part were not given special diets beforehand or the duration of the studies may have been too short . 
005000000000000000000000000000000000000

The six-month trial was funded by the British Heart Foundation and Lichtwer Pharma GmbH , which makes Kwai brand garlic tablets . 
0000000122012200070000

The study did not address whether whole garlic could affect cholesterol . 
000000000000

05700700

Andrew Gray 
34

HAMBURG , Germany 1996-08-22 
5050

A Hamburg court sentenced U.S. neo-Nazi leader Gary Lauck on Thursday to four years in prison for pumping banned extremist propaganda into Germany from his base in the United States . 
0500570340000000000000500000560

Lauck , from Lincoln , Nebraska , yelled a tirade of abuse at the court after his conviction for inciting racial hatred . 
30050500000000000000000

" The struggle will go on , " the 43-year-old shouted in German before being escorted out by security guards . 
000000000000700000000

Lauck 's lawyer vowed he would appeal against the court 's decision , arguing that his client should have been set free because he had not committed any offence under German law . 
300000000000000000000000000000700

The German government hailed the conviction as a major victory in the fight against neo-Nazism . 
0700000000000070

Lauck 's worldwide network has been the main source of anti-Semitic propaganda material flowing into Germany since the 1970s . 
30000000007000050000

" Lauck possessed a well-oiled propaganda machine , honed during more than 20 years , " presiding judge Guenter Bertram told the court . 
030000000000000000340000

" He set up a propaganda cannon and fired it at Germany . " 
00000000000500

said Bertram , who also read out extracts from Lauck 's material praising Hitler as " the greatest of all leaders " and describing the Nazi slaughter of millions of Jews as a myth . 
03000000030003000000000007000070000

Eager to put Lauck behind bars quickly and avoid a long and complex trial , prosecutor Bernd Mauruschat limited his charges to offences since 1994 . 
00030000000000003400000000

He had demanded a five-year jail term but said he was satisfied with the court 's sentence . 
000000000000000000

Publishing and distributing neo-Nazi material is illegal in Germany but Lauck 's defence team had argued that U.S freedom of speech laws meant he was free to produce his swastika-covered books , magazines , videos and flags in his homeland . 
00070000503000000500000000000000000000000

Interior Minister Manfred Kanther said in a statement he " welcomed the prosecution and conviction of one of the ringleaders of international neo-Nazism and biggest distributers of vicious racist publications " . 
00340000000000000000007000000000

" It is high time he was behind bars , " the opposition Social Democrats said in a statement . 
00000000000007800000

Lauck , dressed in a sober blue suit and sporting his trademark Hitleresque black moustache , showed no sign of emotion as Bertram spent more than an hour reading out the verdict and explaining the court 's decision . 
300000000000700000000030000000000000000

But as Lauck was about to be led away , he turned to reporters and blurted out a virtually incomprehensible quick-fire diatribe against the court . 
00300000000000000000000000

" Neither the National Socialists ( Nazis ) nor the communists dared to kidnap an American citizen , " he shouted , in an oblique reference to his extradition to Germany from Denmark . " 
00078070000000070000000000000050500

That 's the truth . " 
000000

His attorney , Hans-Otto Sieg , told reporters outside the courtroom that the judges had not explained how a German court could judge someone for actions carried out in the United States . 
000340000000000000070000000000560

Bertram said Lauck was obsessed by Nazism and devoted his life to leading his National Socialist German Workers ' Party Foreign Organisation ( NSDAP-AO ) , which derives its name from the full German title of Hitler 's Nazi party . 
30300070000000122222220100000000070030700

During the three-month trial , the court dealt mainly with issues of the NSDAP-AO 's " NS Kampfruf " ( " National Socialist Battle Cry " ) magazine , filled with references to Aryan supremacy and defamatory statements about Jews . 
00000000000001001200012220000000070000070

The court rejected Sieg 's argument that Lauck 's extradition from Denmark , where he was arrested in March last year at the request of German authorities , was illegal . 
0003000300050000000000000700000

Lauck was also convicted of disseminating the symbols of anti-constitutional organisations . 
300000000000

He will probably be free in around two and a half years . 
0000000000000

The court ruled that the 15 months he has spent in custody since his arrest should be subtracted from his prison term .

Mother Teresa devoted to world 's poor . 
34000000

CALCUTTA 1996-08-22 
50

Mother Teresa , known as the Saint of the Gutters , won the Nobel Peace Prize in 1979 for bringing hope and dignity to millions of poor , unwanted people with her simple message : " The poor must know that we love them . " 
3400003444000788000000000000000000000000000000

While the world heaps honours on her and even regards her as a living saint , the nun of Albanian descent maintains she is merely doing God 's work . 
000000000000000000070000003000

" It gives me great joy and fulfilment to love and care for the poor and neglected , " she said . " 
00000000000000000000000

The poor do not need our sympathy and pity . 
0000000000

They need our love and compassion . " 
00000000

The diminutive Roman Catholic missionary was on respiratory support in intensive care in an Indian nursing home on Thursday after suffering heart failure . 
007800000000007000000000

But an attending doctor said Mother Teresa , who turns 86 next Tuesday , was conscious and in stable condition . 
000003400000000000000

The task Mother Teresa began alone in 1949 in the slums of densely-populated Calcutta , and grew to touch the hearts of people around the world . 
003400000000050000000000000

When in 1979 she was told she had won the Nobel Peace Prize , she said characteristically : " I am unworthy . " 
000000000078800000000000

The world disagreed , showering more than 80 national and international honours on her including the Bharat Ratna , or Jewel of India , the country 's highest civilian award . 
0000000000000000780078800000000

Her health began to deteriorate in 1989 when she was fitted with a heart pacemaker . 
0000000000000000

A year later , the Vatican announced she was stepping down as Superior of her Missionaries of Charity order . 
00000500000000012200

More than 100 delegates flew in from around the world to elect a successor . 
000000000000000

They could not agree , so asked her to stay on . 
000000000000

She agreed . 
000

In 1991 , Mother Teresa was treated at a California hospital for heart disease and bacterial pneumonia . 
000340000500000000

In 1993 , she fell in Rome and broke three ribs . 
000000500000

In August the same year , while in New Delhi to receive yet another award , she developed malaria , complicated by her heart and lung problems . 
0000000056000000000000000000

Last April she fractured her left collar bone . 
000000000

But her increasing frailty , arthritis and failing eyesight has not stopped her travels around the world to mingle with the poor and desperate . 
0000000000000000000000000

Mother Teresa was born Agnes Goinxha Bejaxhiu to Albanian parents in Skopje , in what was then Serbia , on August 27 , 1910 . 
3400344070050000050000000

She attended a government school and was already deeply religious by the time she was 12 . 
00000000000000000

At the age of 18 she became a Loretto nun , hoping to work at the Order 's Calcutta mission . 
000000007000000000500

She was sent to Loretto Abbey in Dublin and from there to India to begin her novitiate and teach geography at a convent school in Calcutta . 
000056050000500000000000050

She said her divine call to work among the poor came in September , 1946 . " 
00000000000000000

The message was quite clear , " she told one interviewer . " 
0000000000000

I was to leave the convent and help the poor while living among them . 
000000000000000

It was an order . 
00000

I knew where I belonged . " 
0000000

The Vatican and the mother superior in Dublin approved and after intensive training as a nurse with American missionaries she opened her first Calcutta slum school in December 1949 . 
050000050000000007000005000000

She took the name of Teresa , after France 's Saint Therese of the Child Jesus . 
00000300500300030

In India she was simply called Mother . 
05000030

Mother Teresa set up her first home for the dying in a Hindu rest house in Calcutta after she saw a penniless woman turned away by a city hospital . 
340000000000700050000000000000

Named " Nirmal Hriday " ( Tender Heart ) , it was the first of a chain of 150 homes for dying , destitute people , admitting nearly 18,000 a year . 
00560056000000000000000000000000

Her Missionaries of Charity , a Roman Catholic religious order she founded in 1949 , now runs about 300 homes for unwanted children and the destitute in India and abroad . 
0122007800000000000000000005000

In 1994 a British television documentary called the myth around Mother Teresa a mixture of " hyperbole and credulity " . 
000700000034000000000

Catholics around the world rose to her defence . 
700000000

Ukraine hails peace as marks five-year independence . 
50000000

Rostislav Khotin 
34

KIEV 1996-08-23 
50

Ukraine celebrates five years of independence from Kremlin rule on Saturday , hailing civil and inter-ethnic peace as its main post-Soviet achievement . 
50000005000000000000700

Ukraine 's declaration of independence in 1991 , backed nine-to-one by a referendum in December of that year , effectively dealt a death blow to the Soviet empire and ended more than three centuries of rule from Moscow . 
500000000000000000000000007000000000050

Ukraine , with a Russian community of 11 million people -- the world 's largest outside Russia -- has avoided conflicts like those in Russia 's Chechnya , neighbouring Moldova , and the former Soviet republics of Georgia , Azerbaijan and Tajikistan . 
5000700000000000500000005050050000700505050

" Ukraine 's biggest achievements for five years are the preservation of civil peace and inter-ethnic harmony , " President Leonid Kuchma said in televised statement this week . 
05000000000000000000340000000

" Unlike many other post-Soviet countries we were able to deal with conflict situations in a peaceful and civilised way . " 
0000700000000000000000

But independence was initially accompanied by hyper-inflation and economic collapse , although there are signs of a turnaround . 
0000000000000000000

Inflation -- a hyper-inflationary 10,300 percent a year in 1993 -- was a respectable 0.1 percent a month in June and July and the economy has just begun to grow . 
0000000000000000000000000000000

Kuchma told a solemn ceremony at the Ukraina Palace on Friday that " there was a turning point " in reforms and that he expected a rise in the standard of living in the near future . 
3000000560000000000000000000000000000

" There is no doubt that economic growth has already started , " said Adelbert Knobl , head of the International Monetary Fund 's mission in Ukraine . " 
00000000000000340000122000500

The national bank and the government have every reason to be proud of their efforts . " 
00000000000000000

Central bank officials said on Thursday that a much-postponed hryvna currency would " definitely " be introduced before the end of this year . 
000000000000000000000000

It will replace the interim karbovanets currency , which was introduced at par to the Russian rouble in 1992 but now trades at almost 33 karbovanets per rouble . 
00000000000000070000000000000

Ukraine has repeatedly promised to introduce the hryvna but had to postpone the plans because of economic problems . 
5000000000000000000

Proud of its record in promptly joining both the Council of Europe and NATO 's Partnership for Peace , Ukraine caused a foreign policy wrangle this week , offending China by allowing a Taiwanese minister to appear on a public , if unofficial visit . 
000000000122010788050000000005000700000000000

China cancelled a visit by a top-level delegation in protest . 
50000000000

Kiev 's Foreign Minister Hennady Udovenko said Beijing was overreacting . 
50003405000

But Ukraine , seeing itself as a bridge between Russia and the rapidly Westernising countries of eastern Europe , is looking West as well as East . 
050000000500070005000000000

" The strategic aim of European integration should not in any way damage Ukraine 's interests in post-Soviet areas . 
00000700000005000700

Relations with Russia , which is our main partner , have great importance , " Kuchma said . 
005000000000000300

" But Ukraine cannot be economically oriented on Russia , even though those in some circles push us to do that . " 
00500000500000000000000

Kuchma has said Kiev wants membership of the European Union , associate membership of the Western European Union defence grouping and to move closer to NATO . 
300500001200000122000000010

A message from the West this week from U.S. President Bill Clinton congratulated Ukraine on the anniversary , promising to support market reforms and praising Ukraine as a " stabilising factor " in a united Europe .

Oldest Albania book disappears from Vatican - paper . 
050005000

TIRANA 1996-08-23 
50

A 16th-century document , the earliest complete example of written Albanian , has disappeared from the Vatican archives , an Albanian newspaper said on Friday . 
00000000007000005000700000

Gazeta Shqiptare said the " Book of Mass ' , by Gjon Buzuku , dating from 1555 and discovered in 1740 in a religious seminary in Rome , was the first major document published in the Albanian language . 
120007880003400000000000005000000000700

" We Albanians , sons of Buzuku , believed our language had a written document but now we do not have it any more , " lamented scholar Musa Hamiti , told of the loss by the Vatican library . 
0070007000000000000000000000340000000500

Tirana 's national library has three copies of the " Book of Mass ' . " 
5000000000788000

Russia to clamp down on barter deals . 
50000000

MOSCOW 1996-08-23 
50

Russian officials , keen to cut capital flight , will adopt tight measures to cut barter deals in foreign trade to a minimum , a customs official said on Friday . 
7000000000000000000000000000000

" We have always been concerned about barter deals with other countries , viewing them as a disguised kind of capital flight from Russia , " Marina Volkova , deputy head of the currency department at the State Customs Committee , told Reuters . 
00000000000000000000000500340000000001220010

Volkova said last year goods had been exported under many Russian barter deals , with nothing imported in return . 
30000000007000000000

She said the cost of such unimported goods was $ 1.10 billion in 1995 . 
000000000000000

Barter deals were worth $ 4.9 billion last year , or about eight percent of all Russian exports estimated at $ 61.5 billion , she said . 
000000000000000070000000000

" The cost of exported goods is too often understated , so the actual share of barter deals in Russian exports and the amount of unimported goods may be even higher , " Volkova said . 
000000000000000000070000000000000300

A few days ago Russian President Boris Yeltsin issued a decree on state regulation of foreign barter deals , and Volkova said this " could substantially improve the situation " . 
0000703400000000000030000000000

In line with the decree , which will come into force on November 1 , all Russian barter traders will be obliged to import goods worth the cost of their exports within 180 days . 
00000000000000007000000000000000000

" If traders are late , they will have to pay fines worth the cost of their exported goods , " Volkova said . 
000000000000000000000300

Understating the cost of exported goods could still be a loophole for barter dealers , but Volkova said the authorities are currently " tackling the technicalities of the issue " . 
0000000000000000300000000000000

Barter has always been a feature of the Soviet Union 's foreign trade , but Yeltsin 's decrees liberalising foreign trade in 1991-1992 has given barter a new impetus . 
000000005600000300000000000000

A few years ago , barter deals accounted for up to 25-30 percent of Russian exports because " thousands ( of ) trade companies which popped up preferred barter in the absence of reliable Russian banks and money transfer systems " , Volkova said . 
000000000000007000000000000000000070000000300

" Now many Russian banks are strong and can make various sorts of money tranfers , while incompetent traders are being ousted by more experienced ones . 
000700000000000000000000000

But the current share of barter deals in Russian exports is still high , " she said . 
000000007000000000

-- Dmitry Solovyov , Moscow Newsroom , +7095 941 8520 
0340120000

ATHLETICS - MASTERKOVA BREAKS SECOND WORLD RECORD IN 10 DAYS . 
00300000000

Adrian Warner 
34

BRUSSELS 1996-08-23 
50

Russia 's double Olympic champion Svetlana Masterkova smashed her second world record in just 10 days on Friday when she bettered the mark for the women 's 1,000 metres . 
500703400000000000000000000000

After breaking the world record for the women 's mile in Zurich last Wednesday , the Olympic 800 and 1,500 metres champion clocked two minutes 28.98 seconds over 1,000 at the Brussels grand prix meeting . 
000000000005000070000000000000050000

The Russian ate up the ground in a swift last lap to shave 0.36 seconds off the previous best of 2:29.34 set by Mozambique 's Maria Mutola in the same stadium in August last year . 
070000000000000000000005034000000000

Former world 800 champion Mutola pushed Masterkova all the way , finishing second in 2:29.66 . 
0000303000000000

But it was the Russian who picked up the bonus of $ 25,000 for the historic run in front of a capacity 40,000 crowd . 
0000700000000000000000000

Masterkova dominated the middle-distance races at the recent Atlanta Games following her return to competition this season after a three-year maternity break . 
30000000780000000000000

In her first mile race at the richest meeting in Zurich last Wednesday , she slashed 3.05 seconds off the previous record . 
00000000005000000000000

The record of four minutes , 12.56 seconds in Zurich earned Masterkova a bonus of $ 50,000 plus one kilo of gold . 
00000000050300000000000

After Friday 's performance the Russian will have earned well over $ 100,000 in less than a fortnight , taking her appearance money into account . 
00000700000000000000000000

Brussels organisers had laid a new track for the meeting comparable to the surface at the Atlanta Games but put down on a softer surface . 
50000000000000007800000000

Masterkova clearly enjoyed it . 
30000

Mutola looked threatening in the final 200 metres but the Russian found an extra gear to power home several strides ahead , pointing at the time on the clock with delight as she crossed the line . 
3000000000700000000000000000000000000

ATHLETICS - MITCHELL UPSTAGES TRIO OF OLYMPIC SPRINT CHAMPIONS . 
0030007000

Adrian Warner 
34

BRUSSELS 1996-08-23 
50

American Dennis Mitchell upstaged a trio of past and present Olympic 100 metres champions on Friday with a storming victory at the Brussels grand prix . 
73400000007000000000005000

Sporting his customary bright green outfit , the U.S. champion clocked 10.03 seconds despite damp conditions to take the scalp of Canada 's reigning Olympic champion Donovan Bailey , 1992 champion Linford Christie of Britain and American 1984 and 1988 champion Carl Lewis . 
10000000500000000000050070340003405070000340

Mitchell also beat world and Olympic champion Bailey at the most lucrative meeting in the sport in Zurich last week . 
300007030000000005000

The American , who finished fourth at the Atlanta Games , was fast out of his blocks and held off Bailey 's late burst in the final 20 metres before heading off for a lap of celebration . 
07000000780000000000300000000000000000

The Canadian was second in 10.09 with Lewis third in 10.10 , ahead of Atlanta bronze medallist Ato Boldon who clocked 10.12 in fourth . 
0700000300000050034000000

Christie , competing in what is expected to be his last major international meeting , finished fifth in 10.14 . 
30000000000000000000

Lewis , making a rare appearance in Europe in a sprint race , left the track with a slight limp . 
300000050000000000000

American Olympic high hurdles champion Allen Johnson defied the wet conditions to produce a brilliant 12.92 seconds in the 110 metres race , just 0.01 outside the world record held by Britain 's Colin Jackson . 
780003400000000000000000000000050340

Johnson ran the same time at the U.S. Olympic trials in Atlanta in June to become the second equal fastest hurdler of all time with American Roger Kingdom . 
30000005700500000000000007340

He seemed to relish the new track at the Brussels meeting , dominating the race from start to finish with a slight wind at his back . 
000000000500000000000000000

Jackson , the only man to have run faster , could not live with his speed , taking second in 13.24 seconds . 
30000000000000000000000

The rain was pelting down when the women 's high hurdlers stepped up for their 100 metres race . 
0000000000000000000

But Sweden 's Olympic high hurdles champion Ludmila Engquist , who crashed out of last week 's meeting in Zurich after hitting a hurdle , also kept her footing perfectly to win in a fast 12.60 seconds . 
05070003400000000005000000000000000000

Olympic silver medallist Brigita Bukovec of Slovenia could finish only fifth in the race in 12.95 . 
70034050000000000

Jamaican Commonwealth champion Michelle Freeman took second in 12.77 ahead of Cuban Aliuska Lopez . 
710340000007340

The Zurich fall cost Engquist a shot at a jackpot of 20 one-kg gold bars which can be won by athletes who clinch their events at all of the Golden Four series in Oslo , Zurich , Brussels and Berlin . 
05003000000000000000000000000780050505050

Seven athletes went into Friday 's penultimate meeting of the series with a chance of winning the prize and American men 's 400 metres hurdles champion Derrick Adkins kept his hopes alive in the competition by winning his event in 47.93 . 
000000000000000000070000003400000000000000

American Olympic champion Gail Devers clocked a swift 10.84 seconds on her way to victory in the women 's 100 metres , the second fastest time of the season and 0.10 seconds faster than her winning time in Atlanta . 
7803400000000000000000000000000000000050

Jamaican veteran Merlene Ottey , who beat Devers in Zurich after just missing out on the gold medal in Atlanta after a photo finish , had to settle for third place in 11.04 . 
7034000305000000000500000000000000

American world champion Gwen Torrence , the bronze medallist in Atlanta , was second in 11.00 . 
70034000005000000

It was a costly defeat for Ottey since it threw her out of the race for the Golden Four jackpot . 
000000300000000007800

Colombia , U.S. reach aviation agreement . 
5050000

MIAMI 1996-08-23 
50

The U.S. and Colombian governments reached an agreement that will allow AMR Corp 's American Airlines to operate three round-trip flights between New York and Bogota , the Department of Transportation said Friday . 
0507000000012012000000560500122000

Under the agreement , which followed talks in Miami this week , AMR also will be allowed to shift up to four of the weekly flights it now operates between Miami and Colombia to its New York gateway . 
000000005000100000000000000000505005600

The United States also will be able to designate one new all-cargo carrier for service between the two nations after two years . 
05600000000000000000000

Colombia was permitted to add a single additional round-trip flight to its current New York service , although it will not be able to do so while under Category Two ( Conditional ) status under the Federal Aviation Administration 's International Aviation Safety program . 
500000000000056000000000000000000000122078880

Colombia would be allowed to add new service when its safety assessment has been improved , the department said . 
50000000000000000000

With the exception of the new services just agreed to , the governments of the two nations have agreed to maintain their current level of routes and airlines for the next 2-1/2 years , the agreement said . 
00000000000000000000000000000000000000

The agreement resolved a dispute that arose in June when Colombia turned down American 's request to operate flights between New York and Bogota , a denial that prompted the United States to charge that the Colombians were breaking a bilateral aviation agreement and to propose sanctions against one of two Colombian airlines , Avianca and ACES . 
0000000000500100000056050000005600007000000000000007001010

Soccer - Arab team breaks new ground in Israel . 
0070000050

Ori Lewis 
34

TAIBE , Israel 1996-08-23 
5050

For the first time in Israeli history , an Arab team will take the field when the National League soccer season starts on Saturday . 
0000070007000000078000000

Hapoel Taibe fields four Jewish players and two foreign imports -- a Pole and a Romanian . 
12007000000070070

The rest of the side is made up mainly of Moslem Arabs . 
0000000000780

The club , founded in 1961 , has a loyal following in Taibe , an Arab town of 28,000 in the heart of Israel . 
0000000000005007000000050

But away from their home ground , they face unfriendly crowds who taunt the players with racist abuse . 
0000000000000000000

" The very first thing we thought about after we knew we would be promoted was the game against Betar Jerusalem , " said Taibe supporter Karem Haj Yihye . 
000000000000000000012000103440

Two weeks ago Taibe , coached by Pole Wojtek Lazarek , met Betar , a club closely associated with the right-wing Likud party , for the first time in a Cup match in Jerusalem . 
00010007340010000000010000000070050

Chants from the crowd of " Death to the Arabs " , and bottle-throwing during the game marred the match which ended in a goalless draw . 
000000000700000000000000000

One Taibe supporter required hospital treatment for cuts and bruises after a stone struck his head as he was driving from the stadium . 
010000000000000000000000

" We 're used to hearing the taunts of " Death to the Arabs ' , " said Sameh Haj Yihye , a Taibe resident who studies at Jerusalem 's Hebrew University . " 
0000000000000700003440050000501200

But we know that these are only words , nobody has died from hearing them and it only makes us support our team more vehemently . " 
000000000000000000000000000

The dusty town of Taibe lacks the amenities of Jewish communities and many Israeli Arabs have long complained of state discrimination . 
0000500007000780000000

" There are no parks or empty areas of land around here , so when we want to play a friendly game of soccer we all load up in the car and travel to Tel Aviv , " 60 km ( 36 miles ) away , Sameh Haj Yihye said . 
000000000000000000000000000000000056000000000034400

The town 's ramshackle 2,500-seat ground is accessible only by two dirt tracks . 
00000000000000

" We plan to build a 10,000-seat stadium , but it may well be situated elsewhere , " said club chairman Abdul Rahman Haj Yihye . " 
000000000000000000000344400

We will discuss this with the mayor and hopefully a new or refurbished ground will be completed by the start of the new year . " 
00000000000000000000000000

In the meantime , Taibe will play all their heavily policed home matches at the Jewish coastal town of Netanya . 
000010000000000700050

" We are Israelis , there is no question about that , " said Karem Haj Yihye , a hotel waiter . 
0007000000000034400000

" We do n't have any connection with the Palestinians , they live over there , " he said , pointing to the West Bank seven km ( four miles ) to the east . 
00000000070000000000000560000000000

" We do n't feel our club represents Palestinian Arabs , " said club chairman Abdul Rahman . " 
0000000078000003400

We are trying to do all we can to run a professional outfit , we are pleased at any support we get , but do not go out looking to represent the whole Arab world . " 
0000000000000000000000000000000007000

70700500

GROZNY , Russia 1996-08-23 
5050

Rebel fighters and Russian soldiers said a ceasefire effective at noon ( 0800 GMT ) on Friday was being generally observed , although scattered gunfire echoed through the Chechen capital Grozny . 
00070000000007000000000000007050

The Russian army said earlier it was preparing to withdraw from the rebel-dominated southern mountains of the region as part of the peace deal reached with separatists on Thursday . 
070000000000000000000000000000

" There has been some shooting from their side but it has been relatively quiet , " said fighter Aslan Shabazov , a bearded man wearing a white t-shirt and camoflage trousers . 
000000000000000000034000000000000

Soon after he spoke another burst of gunfire rocked the courtyard where the rebels had set up their base and a captured Russian T-72 tank roared out to investigate . 
000000000000000000000077000000

The separatists , who swept into Grozny on August 6 , still control large areas of the centre of town , and Russian soldiers are based at checkpoints on the approach roads . 
000000500000000000000070000000000

" The ceasefire is being observed , " said woman soldier Svetlana Goncharova , 35 , short dark hair poking out from under a peaked camouflage cap . 
0000000000034000000000000000

A few helicopters flew overhead , firing off flares , but there was no shooting from the air . 
0000000000000000000

The truce , the latest of several , was agreed in talks on Thursday between Russian peacemaker Alexander Lebed and rebel chief-of-staff Aslan Maskhadov . 
0000000000000007034000340

The two also agreed to set up joint patrols in Grozny , but Goncharova said she was sceptical about whether this could work . 
000000000050030000000000

" We have to try it , but I doubt if this is possible with the separatists , " she said .

0070000000

LONDON 1996-08-23 
50

Implied volatility of European bond and interest rate options should stabilise around current levels until early next week after falling before and after this week 's German-led cut in interest rates , traders said . 
00070000000000000000000000700000000

" Volatility has come off a lot . 
00000000

We 're looking for it to stabilise now , " said one Euromark options trader at a U.S. bank . 
00000000000070000500

A trader at a Japanese bank said Euromark volatility now stood at 14.00 for September contract , 16.75 for December , 19.50 for March and 21.25 for June . 
00007007000000000000000000000

This compared with midweek levels , before the welter of interest rate cuts , of 18.50 for September , 20.00 for December , 22.00 for March and 23.5 for June , he said . 
0000000000000000000000000000000000

At 1347 GMT , December Euromark futures were trading at 96.78 , two basis points down on the day . 
00700700000000000000

He said the sell-off in June vols might have been overdone , which could offer value at current levels . 
00000000000000000000

He said caps and floors would be well bid after the round of interest rate cuts due to the fact these rates should stay low at the short end . 
000000000000000000000000000000

The size of the Bundesbank 's repo rate cut , to 3.00 percent from 3.30 percent , took markets by surprise . 
0000100000000000000000

" Volatility has a bid to it -- longer-dated volatility more than short-dated because the event people were buying for has passed and now perhaps people will sell some short dated vol and buy some long dated vol , " he said . 
0000000000000000000000000000000000000000000

" Long dated volatility has been low this year , so it is still at levels which are not historically high . 
0000000000000000000000

" It is not a dangerous level to own vol. You are not going to lose a lot and you could make quite a bit . " 
000000000000000000000000000

He said volatility levels should be stable until markets reassess the situation after a long weekend in Britain . 
0000000000000000050

Paribas Capital Markets OTC options specialist Robert Coughlan said that if volatility continued lower for the rest of Friday in over-the-counter 10-year Bunds , it should be higher next Tuesday . 
1222003400000000000000700000000

He said the absence on holiday of many market makers was a main factor behind falls this week in volatility in high-yielding markets such as Italy , Spain and Sweden . 
0000000000000000000000000505050

Coughlan said the market had more downside than upside potential , but a fall was not likely to be of significant size . 
30000000000000000000000

" I recommend people sell strangles in a number of markets -- in Germany and France in particular . 
0000000000000505000

" With high-yielding markets Italy will be a lot more vulnerable in September on economic and political fronts , so I would use current the low level of vol to buy options . 
000050000000000000000000000000000

" So sell options on Bunds and France to enhance yield and buy options on Italy , " Coughlan said ..

Huge Windows 95 sales fail to meet expectations . 
078000000

Martin Wolk 
34

SEATTLE 1996-08-22 
50

A year after its massively publicized introduction , Microsoft Corp. 's Windows 95 computer operating system has fallen short of the most optimistic expectations for the software giant and the industry . 
00000000120780000000000000000000

Even though more than 40 million copies of Windows 95 have been sold , making it the fastest-selling new software ever , it would have been impossible for any product to live up to the unprecedented hype of the Aug. 24 , 1995 launch , when stores around the world opened at midnight to greet long lines of customers . 
000000007800000000000000000000000000000000000000000000000000

The Redmond , Wash.-based company spent tens of millions of dollars promoting the product with stunts that included buying the entire print run of the Times of London and lighting New York 's Empire State building in a Windows color scheme . 
030700000000000000000000012200560560007000

But the product , delivered eight months late , has fallen short of its sales potential in part because Microsoft delivered a mixed message to business customers , analysts said . 
0000000000000000000100000000000

" It did n't do as well as it could have , " said Rob Enderle , an analyst with Giga Information Group . 
000000000000003400001220

Scores of software and hardware companies that had hoped for a big boost in sales were disappointed when only a brief spike materialized . 
000000000000000000000000

" People who were expecting major coat-tails were somewhat disappointed , " said Scott Winkler , an analyst with Gartner Group . 
0000000000000340000120

" It 's not as though it has n't had an impact , " he said . " 
000000000000000000

It just has n't had the huge earth-shattering impact some people were looking for . " 
0000000000000000

Symantec Corp. , which had been among the most bullish of software companies at the time of the Windows 95 launch , ended up posting disappointing financial results when retail sales of the operating system fell short of its projections . 
12000000000000000078000000000000000000000

Touchstone Software Corp. had to pay $ 1.3 million in cash and stock to settle a shareholders lawsuit brought after the company 's sales failed to meet expectations tied to the Windows 95 launch . 
12200000000000000000000000000007800

Many software developers apparently saw their crucial holiday season sales suffer last year because store shelves were jammed with blue-and-white boxes of Windows 95 , resulting in a shortage of space for seasonal products , said Ann Stephens , president of PC Data Inc . 
000000000000000000000078000000000000340001220

To be sure , sales of Windows 95 and the accompanying Office 95 upgrade drove Microsoft sales up 46 percent last year to a record $ 8.67 billion and cemented the company 's status as the industry 's dominant company . 
00000078000780010000000000000000000000000

Microsoft executives say they are thrilled with the sales figures , and industry analysts estimate that by sometime next year , the installed base of Windows 95 will surpass that of the older version of Windows , now used on about 100 million computers worldwide . 
1000000000000000000000000780000000070000000000

But Enderle said the figure could have been even higher if Microsoft had done a better job of handling the huge demand for technical support from customers who were frustrated trying to install the system . 
030000000001000000000000000000000000

He and other analysts said corporate America adopted a go-slow approach because Microsoft already was promoting the new version of its high-end Windows NT operating system , expected to be available in stores in the next several weeks . 
000000500000100000000078000000000000000

" Microsoft sent a lot of signals that NT was going to be the answer , " Winkler said . " 
010000007000000003000

Many people began to believe that Windows 95 was being downplayed . " 
0000007800000

But now that Windows NT 4.0 has been launched , Winkler and others believe only a relatively small proportion of corporate users will elect to pay the added software and hardware costs needed to use it instead of Windows 95 . 
00078800003000000000000000000000000000780

" Windows 95 is going to do great , " he said . " 
07800000000000

The mistake people made was in thinking it was going to be a fast , sweeping change rather than a slow , building change . "

China copper stocks owned by state reserve - trade . 
5000000000

Lynne O'Donnell 
34

HONG KONG 1996-08-23 
560

Up to 100,000 tonnes of copper held in Shanghai bonded warehouses , confounding the world market as to its source and ultimate fate , probably belongs to China 's strategic state reserve , industry sources said on Friday . 
000000005000000000000000000500000000000

Around 40,000 tonnes of the copper have already been moved to warehouses near the northern port of Yingkou , where some of the strategic stockpile was stored , they said . 
0000000000000000050000000000000

Just who owns the copper is a question that has kept traders and industry analysts guessing since the metal was channelled into Shanghai by the China National Nonferrous Metals Import and Export Corp ( CNIEC ) in June and July . 
00000000000000000000005001222222201000000

It was unclear whether or not the 40,000 tonnes had cleared customs -- which would provide some concrete indication that the strategic reserve , administered directly by the central government 's State Planning Commission , owned the copper . 
000000000000000000000000000000012200000

Traders have said the reserve could negotiate concessions on duties -- three percent import tax and 17 percent value-added tax -- that made the copper prohibitively expensive otherwise . 
00000000000000000000000000000

But one source , the head of a Hong Kong trading house , said it made no difference if the copper was customs cleared or not . 
000000005600000000000000000

" If they spend all this money moving the copper to Yingkou , it will be sitting there for years , " he said . 
0000000000050000000000000

" Once it arrives in Yingkou , it is subject to monitoring by the State Planning Commission , which has to give permission for any more movement ; it is out of the hands of traders , " he said . 
00000500000000122000000000000000000000000

Mystery has surrounded the Shanghai stockpile in recent months , with traders unsure not only of who owns it , but of its exact size and what its owner planned to do with it . 
00005000000000000000000000000000000

Trading sources generally agreed it would be cost-effective to take the copper back into a depleted central reserve as it had already served its purpose in taking advantage of long-term backwardation on the London Metal Exchange ( LME ) . 
0000000000000000000000000000000001220100

A backwardation occurs when the spot price of a metal is higher than the forward price . 
00000000000000000

CNIEC lent around 85,000 tonnes of copper onto the LME between April and June 1995 on behalf of the state reserve , running the state stockpile down to 115,000 tonnes from 200,000 tonnes previously . 
10000000010000000000000000000000000

Traders in Asia said CNIEC could well have lent it to the market at around US$ 2,700 a tonne , and then paid somewhere between $ 2,200 and $ 2,400 a tonne when it started taking the metal back earlier this year . 
0050100000000007000000000000000000000000000

This would have cleared CNIEC a healthy profit , which could then have been used to finance storage and other costs . 
0000100000000000000000

Word that CNIEC had offered the copper to European trading houses in a series of secret meetings unnerved an already jittery market . 
00100000700000000000000

Industry analysts Bloomsbury Minerals Economics ( BME ) said on Wednesday the motivation of the owners of the 85,000 tonnes , " whoever they are , is the most important short-term fundamental " in an already tight world market . 
0012201000000000000000000000000000000000

BME repeated in its latest review rumours of involvement by Sumitomo Corp , with CNIEC said to be helping the Japanese trader unload its copper positions after it revealed in June losses of $ 1.8 billion in a decade of unauthorised deals . 
1000000000120010000070000000000000000000000

Sumitomo and CNIEC have made no comments on the talk and Chinese traders said they know nothing of such an arrangement . 
1010000000070000000000

Traders in Shanghai said on Thursday they were unaware of movements out of the Shanghai bonded warehouses . 
005000000000005000

They reported more arrivals that were probably spot purchases . 
0000000000

They also expressed concern that the tonnage in bonded warehouses would move onto the domestic market . 
00000000000000000

But these concerns were irrelevant , a Singapore trader said , despite a forecast that domestic Chinese copper demand could hit one million tonnes this year . 
000000050000000070000000000

As with many commodities , " there is a desire ( by the Chinese government ) to keep a stockpile of the metal , " he said . " 
00000000000007000000000000000

You do n't keep it to help industry , you keep it in case of emergency . " 
000000000000000000

-- Hong Kong newsroom ( 852 ) 2843-6470

German retailer Promodes is in advanced talks about selling its German assets and the retailer 's board might decide as soon as Tuesday to sell the assets to Spar AG , Les Echos newspaper said on Friday .

000012200000000007010101000000

100500000000000000000100

07000700000

Ford China JV posts 77 percent net drop in H1 96 . 
120000000000

SHANGHAI 1996-08-24 
50

A Chinese truck maker in which Ford Motor Co has a 20 percent stake said it posted a 77 percent drop in post-tax profits in the first half of 1996 . 
0700001220000000000000000000000

Jiangling Motors Corp , in a statement in Saturday 's edition of the China Securities newspaper , said net profit in the period was 3.385 million yuan , down from 14.956 million in the same 1995 period . 
12200000000001200000000000000000000000

Turnover fell to 937.891 million yuan from 1.215 billion , while net assets per share were 1.88 yuan , unchanged , and earnings per share fell to 0.005 yuan from 0.02 yuan , the statement said . 
0000000000000000000000000000000000000

In the first half , the company said it produced 8,333 vehicles and sold 9,018 , but it did not explain the difference . 
000000000000000000000000

It blamed the drop in profits on a weak vehicle market and said as its engine plant had only just started trial production , the company 's results would not improve in the short-term . 
00000000000000000000000000000000000

Ford owns 138.643 million shares in the firm . 
100000000

The majority shareholder , with 51 percent , or 353.24 million shares , is Jiangling Motors Group . 
000000000000001220

The company , in the southern province of Jiangxi , had about eight percent of China 's light truck market in 1994 . 
00000000500000050000000

( $ 1 = 8.3 yuan )

503400000010000000000000078800000000

On a weekend overshadowed by Friday 's fatal accident , four times world champion Kankunnen emerged from the first five of Saturday 's 10 stages with a commanding advantage over his country 's latest prospect , Marcus Gronholm , also in a Toyota . 
00000000000000300000000000000000000034000010

000340010000003400000000

0000000000000070001000000

00034000003400000

00000000000000

CRICKET - ESSEX POISED TO STEP UP TITLE CHALLENGE . 
0010000000

LONDON 1996-08-24 
50

Essex are set to step up their English county championship challenge with a fifth consecutive victory after new-ball pair Neil Williams and Mark Ilott sent Gloucestershire reeling on Saturday . 
100000070000000000034034010000

Williams seized two wickets in two deliveries and left-armer Ilott also captured two as Gloucestershire , 252 behind on first innings , slumped to 27 for four at the close on the third day of the four-day game at Colchester . 
30000000030000100000000000000000000000050

Essex , who started the current round of matches in fifth place 20 points behind leaders Derbyshire with a game in hand , could go top if they complete victory on Monday 's last day and other results favour them . 
10000000000000001000000000000000000000000

Williams thrust Essex on course for success by dispatching Matt Windows and Andrew Symonds in his second over , before Ilott removed Dominic Hewson and Tim Hancock to reduce Gloucestershire to 17 for four at one stage . 
30100000034034000000303403400100000000

The visitors had started the day optimistically by sending back former England captain Graham Gooch when he added just six to his overnight 105 , but Essex went on to make 532 for eight before declaring . 
0000000000050340000000000010000000000

Captain Paul Prichard plundered 88 from 73 deliveries , hitting 15 fours and one six . 
0340000000000000

Second-placed Kent were frustrated by rain which prevented any play at Cardiff , where they have reached 255 for three in their first innings against Glamorgan , while third-placed Surrey are facing an uphill task against Nottinghamshire . 
01000000000500000000000001000100000010

Surrey slipped to 88 for four in reply to Notts ' commanding first innings of 446 for nine declared at Trent Bridge , before Alistair Brown struck a 55-ball half-century . 
1000000001000000000056003400000

Brown 's 56 not out , containing eight fours and three sixes , lifted Surrey to 128 for four on a rain-curtailed day . 
300000000000001000000000

Fourth-placed Leicestershire had Hampshire on the ropes at Leicester before rain intervened . 
0101000050000

Pace trio David Millns ( 2-24 ) , Gordon Parsons ( 3-20 ) and Vince Wells ( 2-19 ) had Hampshire reeling at 81 for seven in reply to the home county 's first innings of 353 . 
00340000340000340000100000000000000000

Yorkshire rekindled their title hopes after three successive defeats by taking the upper hand against arch-rivals Lancashire at Old Trafford . 
100000000000000010560

Facing Yorkshire 's 529 for eight declared , Lancashire were forced to follow on 206 behind after being bowled out for 323 , paceman Darren Gough polishing off the innings with a burst of three wickets for one run in 17 deliveries . 
0100000010000000000000003400000000000000000

Lancashire then reached 210 for five at the close -- just four ahead -- after Neil Fairbrother hit 55 in 60 balls to add to his first innings of 86 .

RUGBY UNION - NEW ZEALAND WIN FIRST SERIES IN SOUTH AFRICA . 
120560000560

PRETORIA , South Africa 1996-08-24 
50560

New Zealand made history on Saturday when they completed their first series victory in South Africa with a 33-26 victory in the second test . 
5600000000000056000000000

The win gave the All Blacks an unbeatable 2-0 lead in the three-test series . 
000012000000000

Each side scored three tries and the Springboks outscored the All Blacks 15-12 in the second half but still suffered a fourth successive defeat against their old enemies . 
00000001001200000000000000000

Two tries from wing Jeff Wilson in the first quarter gave New Zealand a 24-11 lead before tries from flanker Ruben Kruger and scrum-half Joost van der Westhuizen in the space of two minutes narrowed the gap to a single point at 23-24 . 
00003400000560000000340034440000000000000000

The Springboks would have gone ahead had not fly-half Joel Stransky 's conversion hit an upright and New Zealand only scrambled to safety through a fine penalty from replacement fly-half Jon Preston and a drop goal by number eight Zinzan Brooke . 
010000000340000005600000000000340000000340

SOCCER - DISAPPOINTING AJAX SLUMP 2-0 AT HEERENVEEN . 
000100050

AMSTERDAM 1996-08-24 
50

Dutch champions Ajax Amsterdam faltered in their second league match of the season on Saturday losing 2-0 away at Heerenveen . 
701200000000000000010

Ajax , who had a dismal series of pre-season results before beating NAC of Breda in their opening game , had the best of an entertaining first half but failed to break the deadlock . 
10000000000010500000000000000000000

Eight minutes after the interval , Heerenveen 's Romeo Wouden broke through the Amsterdam defence , left defender John Veldman standing and curled the ball beyond goalkeeper Edwin van der Sar into the Ajax net . 
000000103400050000340000000344400100

Ajax , without injured defenders Marcio Santos and Winston Bogarde and strikers Jari Litmanen and Marc Overmars , then stepped up the pace and looked certain to equalise . 
10000340340034034000000000000

But they left gaps at the back and on 73 minutes Danish striker Jon Dahl Tomasson rushed out of his own half , beat the Ajax defence and lobbed van der Sar . 
000000000007034400000000010003440

The defeat means Ajax 's main title contenders PSV Eindhoven , who beat the champions 3-0 in the traditional league curtain-raiser , can go three points clear of their rivals if they beat Groningen on Sunday . 
0001000012000000000000000000000001000

British hostage in Chechnya describes ordeal . 
7005000

LONDON 1996-08-24 
50

A British aid worker , held hostage in Chechnya for nearly four weeks , said on Saturday a cocked Kalashnikov had been thrust into his mouth at one point during his ordeal . 
070000005000000000070000000000000

Michael Penrose , a 23-year-old worker with the group Action Against Hunger , described his ordeal to a news conference when he arrived back in Britain from Moscow . 
34000000012200000000000005050

" The worst period of physical manhandling was during that time when we were beaten with Kalashnikovs and at one point I had a Kalashnikov held to the back of my throat -- cocked , " he said . 
000000000000000070000000700000000000000

" For the first period we were held in a small room with no bed or anything . 
000000000000000000

We had very little food and sometimes went two or three days without eating . " 
0000000000000000

Gunmen seized Penrose , who comes from Swerford in southern England , Frenchman Frederic Malardeau and six other hostages from their car in Grozny , the capital of Chechnya , on July 27 . 
0030000500507340000000050000500000

The assailants had demanded a ransom of 300,000 pounds ( $ 465,000 ) but no money was paid by the charity when they were released on Wednesday . 
0000000000000000000000000000

The hostages were held in a house in or near Grozny which was bombarded regularly . 
0000000000500000

" During the last 15 days of being held , the fighting in Grozny was very close . 
000000000000050000

At first it was street fighting outside the house and then we came under very heavy shelling and bombardment from conventional weapons like tanks , artillery and grenade launchers , " he said . 
0000000000000000000000000000000000

Penrose had been working for the charity which provides food to civilians for only a few weeks before he was captured . 
3000000000000000000000

When asked if he would return to the mountainous region where rebels have been fighting Russian troops for full independence , Penrose said : " Not for the time being . 
0000000000000007000003000000000

I do n't think it 's safe for me . 
0000000000

But maybe in the future , depending on the circumstances . " 
000000000000

Princess Diana send message to Mother Teresa . 
03000340

LONDON 1996-08-24 
50

Britain 's Princess Diana has sent a message to seriously ill Mother Teresa , the nun to whom she has turned several times for spiritual guidance . 
500300000003400000000000000

Diana 's office said on Saturday the princess had sent a message to the Nobel Peace Prize-winning missionary as news broke this week of her battle against heart problems and malaria . 
30000000000000788000000000000000

A spokeswoman declined to release details of the message . 
0000000000

Diana first met the Albanian-born missionary in Rome in 1992 . 
30007005000

She said afterwards that the meeting had fulfilled her " dearest wish " and the two women have met several times since . 
00000000000000000000000

The princess , who has carved out a major role for herself as a helper of the sick and needy , is said to have turned to Mother Teresa for guidance as her marriage crumbled to heir to the British throne Prince Charles . 
00000000000000000000000000034000000000070340

The 85-year-old nun said in the past that she was praying for the couple , whose divorce is expected to become final next week . 
0000000000000000000000000

Doctors caring for Mother Teresa in a Calcutta hospital said on Saturday that her fever had fallen and her malaria was under control but she remained on a respirator in intensive care . 
000340050000000000000000000000000
