About 350 adventurers from nine countries set out on Saturday to climb , raft , bike and run in a 323-mile ( 517-km ) endurance race through the Canadian wilderness . 
0000000000000000000000000000700

The event , called the Eco-Challenge , is part of a growing sport known as adventure racing in which competitors test their limits for days over a perilous wilderness course . 
0000070000000000000000000000000

" I 'm looking forward to this race . 
000000000

I think it will be more physically challenging and we 'll have to go up against more diverse situations due to the terrain , " said Dr. Michael Stroud , a veteran Eco-Challenge participant . 
00000000000000000000000000034000700

The Eco-Challenge has been staged twice before -- in Utah and Maine last year -- and is modelled on similar races overseas . 
07000000050500000000000

The 70 teams in this year 's race will will trek glaciers , climb mountains , whitewater raft , horseback ride , canoe and mountain bike along the grueling course . 
0000000000000000000000000000000

This year 's race , the route of which was keep a secret until Friday evening , is being held near Pemberton , British Columbia , about 100 miles ( 160 km ) northeast of Vancouver . 
0000000000000000000005056000000000050

The area is filled with treacherous mountain peaks , ice fields and frigid waters . 
000000000000000

Organisers expect about two-thirds of the participants to drop out or be disqualified before the finish . 
00000000000000000

The hardy ones are expected to complete the course in about six days , with first-place finishers receiving $ 10,000 in prize money . 
000000000000000000000000

In the Eco-Challenge , competitors race in teams of five which must include both men and women . 
007000000000000000

Team members must remain within 100 yards ( metres ) of each other at all times and finish together . 
00000000000000000000

With racers carrying about 40 pounds ( 18 kg ) of gear on their backs , broken bones , sunstroke , dehydration and exhaustion are common .

30000000

Laurence McQuillan 
34

WASHINGTON 1996-08-24 
50

President Bill Clinton has served notice he intends to be busy " making news " -- or at least doing things that look and sound like it in a campaign year . 
03400000000000000000000000000000

With Democrats gathering in Chicago to start a convention on Monday to nominate him for a second term as president , Clinton plans a steady parade of events designed to highlight his leadership and dim the glow of the just-concluded Republican conclave that gave a boost to rival Bob Dole . 
070050000000000000000300000000000000000070000000340

After a week of carefully orchestrated events signing into law bills passed by the Republican-controlled Congress , Clinton used his Saturday radio address to the nation to proudly " announce " a development in the war on crime . 
000000000000007103000000000000000000000

" Sixty days ago I directed the attorney general to draw up a plan for a national registry of sex offenders , " Clinton said . " 
000000000000000000000003000

That plan has now reached my desk . " 
000000000

" Today I am pleased to announce that we are following through on our commitment to keep track of these criminals , not just in a single state but wherever they go , " he said . 
0000000000000000000000000000000000000

Actually , creation of such a registry was underway without Clinton lifting a finger . 
000000000030000

Attorney General Janet Reno 's report -- all nine pages of it , including footnotes -- offers only the interim services of the FBI until a formal registry on sex offenders has been established . 
00340000000000000000000100000000000

Two months ago , Clinton announced he wanted an interim effort established . 
0000300000000

Now , 60 days later , he had a chance to talk about it again . 
0000000000000000

It is an example of Clinton 's strategic planning as he heads into the stretch drive for the Nov. 5 presidential election . 
00000300000000000000000

Such things do not happen by chance in the Clinton White House , they are part of his political chess game . 
0000000003560000000000

In the past week Clinton signed into law an increase in the minimium wage , a bill that makes it easier for someone with a pre-existing health problem to change jobs , and sweeping changes overhauling the nation 's welfare system . 
000030000000000000000000000000000000000000

" America can look back on a week of remarkable achievement , " Clinton said , without even a passing reference to the Republican majority in the House and Senate . 
0500000000000300000000070001010

" America is on the right track offering more opportunity , demanding more responsibility , building a stronger community , the sense of shared values and stronger families , " he said in striking the theme of his coming week . 
05000000000000000000000000000000000000000

According to a senior campaign official , Clinton " will be making a lot of news in the coming week -- something different each day . " 
000000030000000000000000000

Clinton departs on Sunday on a four-day train trip through West Virginia , Kentucky , Ohio , Michigan and Indiana while fellow Democrats are gathered in Chicago . 
3000000000560505050500700050

" He 'll make news during the day ... and then at night the attention will go to the convention , " said the campaign official . " 
0000000000000000000000000000

We think it 'll work really well . " 
000000000

Although officials decline to say just what each day 's " news " will be , the intent is to put a focus on Clinton himself and not just those attending the party 's convention . 
000000000000000000000000300000000000

Each day of the trip will have a late start , so that network television correspondents will be able to do live reports for morning programmes . 
000000000000000000000000000

Campaign officials then hope the day 's " news " event will be showcased on evening television news shows as a lead-in for that night 's convention programme . 
00000000000000000000000000000

" We 'll be concentrating ... on supporting the president as he is on the trip and making significant public policy statements related to some of his plans for the future , " said White House Press Secretary Mike McCurry . 
00000000000000000000000000000000005600340

McCurry said that when Clinton delivers his acceptance address on Thursday night to fellow Democrats and a national television audience , he will " set out a road map " for the nation 's future -- one the president hopes guides him back to the White House for four more years .

They put forward no proof to support the speculation , but seized on a comment by chief prosecutor Michel Bourlet on Belgian television on Friday night that he would chase down everyone involved in the case " if I am allowed to " . 
00000000000000000034070000000000000000000000

Bourlet said between 300 and 400 paedophile porn video tapes had been seized , some of which featured Dutroux . 
30000000000000000030

Dutroux was charged a week ago after police rescued two young girls from a concrete dungeon in the basement of one of the six houses he owns in and around Charleroi . 
30000000000000000000000000000050

Just a day later the national euphoria at the rescue turned to disgust as Dutroux led police to the bodies of two eight-year-old girls in another of his houses . 
000000000000003000000000000000

Julie Lejeune and Melissa Russo , had been kidnapped in June last year . 
34034000000000

Dutroux said they starved to death nine months later . 
3000000000

He also admitted kidnapping two other girls , An Marchal and Eefje Lambrecks , a year ago . 
000000003403400000

The fate of the girls is unknown , but there has been speculation they were sold into prostitution in Slovakia or the Czech Republic where Dutroux was a frequent visitor . 
0000000000000000000500560300000

Belgian police have visited Bratislava and will visit Prague . 
7000500050

Five other people have been arrested including Dutroux 's second wife Michelle Martin , charged as an accomplice . 
0000000300034000000

The others have been charged with abduction and illegal imprisonment of children or are suspected of criminal association . 
0000000000000000000

Dutch police are also holding a 74-year old Dutchman in connection with the disappearance of An and Eefje , although a spokesman said no direct link had yet been established . 
7000000070000003030000000000000

At least part of the speculation in the Belgian media of high-level protection for Dutroux and his accomplices is based on leaked documents cataloguing a high degree of police bungling , incompetence and indifference . 
00000000700000300000000000000000000

Among the revelations are the fact that the gendarmerie was running a surveillance operation codenamed " Othello " against Dutroux in 1995 -- when both Julie and Melissa and An and Eefje were kidnapped . 
00000000000000007003000003030303000

They show that the gendarmes were aware that Dutroux was building cells in some of his houses for holding children , yet this information was either not passed on to other police forces searching for the missing girls or was overlooked when it was . 
000000003000000000000000000000000000000000000

They also show that police investigating a theft visited Dutroux late last year at the house where Julie and Melissa were being held but accepted his word that the children 's cries they could hear came from neighbours . 
000000000300000003030000000000000000000

Justice Minister Stefaan De Clerck has admitted that mistakes were made and ordered an inquiry at the same time as stressing there were no indications of a cover-up . 
10344000000000000000000000000

There is also widespread disbelief that no one appeared to question how Dutroux , an unemployed father of three with no visible means of support , managed to own six houses . 
00000000000030000000000000000000

0700000000000000000000000005000

7000000000000000000000000000005600000000050

The security forces also said a man carrying an explosive device also died after it went off prematurely .

El-Watan paper said the blast killed seven -- a mother and her 25-year-old daughter , four young boys and a five-year-old girl . 
10000000000000000000000

Several people were also wounded , it said . 
000000000

00000000000500000

000012220000000000000000000070000000

An estimated 50,000 Algerians and more than 110 foreigners have been killed in violence pitting Moslem rebels against government forces since early 1992 , when the authorities cancelled a general election in which radical Islamists had taken a commanding lead .

Most Spaniards back talks with Basque rebels--poll .

MADRID 1996-08-24 
50

Most Spaniards would support government talks with the illegal Basque separatist group ETA if the rebels renounced violence permanently , a survey published in daily El Mundo on Saturday said . 
0000000007001000000000000120000

While 57 percent of the population supported negotiations with ETA ( Basque Homeland and Freedom ) , 30 percent opposed it , the survey by the state-controlled Centre for Sociological Studies ( CIS ) found . 
000000000101222000000000000122201000

But 80 percent said ETA had shown little interest in achieving peace in the Basque country when it offered a one-week truce in July while continuing to hold prison officer Jose Antonio Ortega Lara , kidnapped in January . 
000010000000007000000000000000344400000

The problem of terrorism had neither worsened nor improved since the conservative Popular Party ( PP ) came to power in May , according to 56 percent of those questioned , while 22 percent said it had worsened . 
000000000000120100000000000000000000000

The survey questioned 2,496 people between July 17 and 21 and has a margin of error of plus or minus two percent .

50

At least 30 people have been killed and about 100 injured in the flood-hit Pakistani city of Lahore , newspapers reported on Saturday . 
000000000000007005000000

00000000000005000000000000000000000000000000000

Newspapers quoted witnesses as saying they had seen bodies floating in the streets .

Among the dead were five members of the religious Jamaat-i-Islami party who drowned while trying to remove books from a basement library .

They said thousands of people had been made homeless after a breach opened in the city canal , inundating residential areas .

Army troops were called in to evacuate residents of low-lying areas to higher ground . 
000000000000000

Officials said the Ravi and Chenab rivers , which both flow through Punjab , were in high flood and emergency services backed by troops were on full alert .

Internet Startup funded to develop Java software . 
12000700

MOUNTAIN VIEW , Calif. 1996-08-25 
56050

A small team of engineers from Sun Microsystems Inc. 's JavaSoft unit said Sunday they have formed a new company , dubbed Internet Startup , to build Java infrastructure software . 
0000001220100000000000120007000

The fledgling company , established in a ground-floor office here over the last two weeks , has received venture financing from Bessemer Venture Partners of Menlo Park , Calif .. 
000000000000000000000122056050

David Cowan , Internet Startup founder and acting chief executive , is a general partner of Bessemer . 
340120000000000010

The startup company 's acting chairman is Jim Bidzos , the president of RSA Data Security , a unit of Security Dynamics Technologies Inc. as well as chairman of VeriSign . 
0000000340000122000012220000010

Internet Startup , which opened its doors with about half a dozen initial employees , combines experience at JavaSoft , Apple Computer Inc. , and Oracle Systems . 
1200000000000000001012200120

" Java portends dramatic changes in the way we use the Internet , " said Hong Bui , vice president of engineering of the new company after serving as a senior engineer at JavaSoft . 
07000000000700034000000000000000010

Java is a computer programming language introduced by Sun Microsystems in mid-1995 which has immediately captured the attention of the industry for its ability to operate across virtually all computer system in a relatively secure manner . 
7000000012000000000000000000000000000

Just last week , Sun Microsystems and the Silicon Valley venture capital giant Kleiner Perkins Caufield & Byers said they had completed financing of a $ 100 million fund managed by Kleiner Perkins to fund startups developing Java technologies . 
0000120056000122220000000000000120000700

Java has been licensed by nearly 50 organisations , ranging from Microsoft Corp. and International Business Machines Corp. to the Taiwan government . 
70000000000120122200500

Prasad Wagle , another former senior JavaSoft engineer who is among the founding engineers at Internet Startup , said the new company aims to build software infrastructure using Java to make networked applications ubiquitious . 
34000010000000012000000000007000000

One feature of the Java language is that small software programmes , known as " applets " because they are small applications , can be downloaded from the server computers at the centre of networks onto individual computers for use . 
00007000000000000000000000000000000000000

In this model , individual computer users can always gain access to the latest programmes and do not need to store more software than they are currently using on their computers at any one time , also saving costs of memory and storage . 
00000000000000000000000000000000000000000000

Chris Zuleeg , a veteran of Apple and a former JavaSoft marketing manager , is vice president of marketing at Internet Startup , whose Web site is www.internetstartup.com . 
34000010001000000000120000000

Bessemer has funded numerous Internet pioneers , including PSI Net , VeriSign and Individual . 
100070001201010

GOLF - MICKELSON WINS FOURTH TITLE OF YEAR IN AKRON . 
00300000050

AKRON , Ohio 1996-08-25 
5050

Phil Mickelson birdied two of the last three holes to win World Series of Golf by three strokes over Billy Mayfair on Sunday . 
340000000007888000034000

It was the fourth tournament title this year for Mickelson , who shot an even-par 70 , after being tied for the lead with Billy Mayfair with three holes to play . 
00000000030000000000000034000000

Along with Mayfiar at 277 for the tournament were Steve Stricker , who had a 68 , and Duffy Waldorf , with a 66 . 
0030000003400000003400000

" It was very hard to sleep last night because there was so much I could accomplish with this win , " said Mickelson , who had a three-stroke lead entering the third round . " 
000000000000000000000003000000000000

This was a win I wanted very , very much . " 
000000000000

Mickelson 's victory gave him a 10 year exemption to the PGA Tour . 
30000000000780

The $ 378,000 first place check brings Mickelson back to the top of the money list with $ 1,574,799 won this year . 
00000003000000000000000

" This is a major championship golf course , and for me to perform well on this style of course is a big step up for me in my career and my performance in future majors , " he said . 
00000000000000000000000000000000000000000

Mickelson three-stroke lead was cut to two when Mayfair birdied the course 's only easy hole , the par five second hole , while Mickelson three-putted for par from 25 feet . 
30000000300000000000000030000000

On the back nine Mickelson began driving erratically , and poor tee shots resulted in bogeys on the , eighth , 12th and 13th holes , bringing Mickelson back to four under par , tied with Mayfair , who had parred 14 straight holes after the birdie on no.2 . 
00003000000000000000000000030000000030000000000000

Mickelson then set up a tap in birdie on the 16th , sending a wedge shot to 18 inches . 
30000000000000000000

He had another birdie on the 17th , where he his a 6-iron to six feet . 
00000000000000000

Mayfair bogeyed the 17th , missing a five foot par putt , and dropped from solo second place to a three way tie for second . 
30000000000000000000000000

It was the second successive year in which Mayfair has finished runner up in this tournament . 
00000000300000000

He lost to Greg Norman in sudden death last year . 
00034000000

The defending champion was in contention , two behind Mickelson for much of the day , until he bogeyed the 13th and 14th holes .

MOTORCYCLING - JAPANESE WIN BOTH ROUND NINE SUPERBIKE RACES . 
0070003000

SUGO , Japan 1996-08-25 
5050

Teenager Yuuichi Takeda , racing in only his first season , outclassed the big names to win the first race in round nine of the world superbike championship on Sunday . 
0340000000000000000000000000000

Takeda , 18 , showed poise far beyond his years to overtake Australian Ducati rider Troy Corser , last year 's championship runner-up , with four of the 25 laps left . 
30000000000071034000000000000000

Honda 's Takeda was pursued past Corser by the Yamaha duo of Noriyuki Haga and Wataru Yoshikawa with Haga briefly taking the lead in the final chicane on the last lap . 
10300030010034034030000000000000

But Takeda found one more spurt of power to just take the flag first with Haga second and Yoshikawa third . 
030000000000000300300

Haga had the consolation of recording the fastest lap at 147.159 kph . 
3000000000000

Corser , who crashed during practice on Friday , limped in fourth , four seconds behind Takeda with championship leader Aaron Slight of New Zealand 11 seconds behind the winner . 
3000000000000000300034056000000

In the second race , Takeda again challenged strongly until the fifth lap from the end when he crashed while running second to eventual race winner Takuma Aoki . 
00000300000000000000000000340

Aoki , the elder brother of reigning 125cc world champion Haruchika , had a race-long duel with John Kocinski of the United States on a Ducati before taking the chequered flag . 
30000000003000000340056001000000

Kocinski led for the early laps before he was passed first by Aoki , who recorded the fastest lap of 147.786 kph , and then by Takeda . 
3000000000003000000000000030

With Takeda out of the race , Kocinski regained second place but he could not overtake Aoki . 
030000030000000030

Haga again was the unlucky rider finishing third ahead of Slight with Corser in 10th place . 
30000000003030000

But the strong showing by the Japanese riders did not alter the championship table with Slight still leading on 280 points , followed by Corser with 269 and Kocinski with 254 . 
00000070000000030000000030003000

CRICKET - POLLOCK CONCLUDES WARWICKSHIRE CAREER WITH FLOURISH . 
003010000

LONDON 1996-08-25 
50

South African fast bowler Shaun Pollock concluded his Warwickshire career with a flourish on Sunday by taking the final three wickets during the county 's Sunday league victory over Worcestershire . 
7800340010000000000000000000010

Pollock , who returns home on Tuesday for an ankle operation , took the last three wickets in nine balls as Worcestershire were dismissed for 154 . 
300000000000000000000100000

After an hour 's interruption for rain , Warwickshire then reached an adjusted target of 109 with 13 balls to spare and record their fifth win in the last six games . 
00000000100000000000000000000000

Warwickshire are currently in fourth position behind Yorkshire , Nottinghamshire and Surrey . 
1000000101010

Yorkshire captain David Byas completed his third Sunday league century as his side swept clear at the top of the table , reaching a career best 111 not out against Lancashire . 
10340000000000000000000000000010

Lancashire 's total of 205 for eight from 40 overs looked reasonable before Byas put their attack to the sword , collecting his runs from just 100 balls with three sixes and nine fours . 
10000000000003000000000000000000000

Yorkshire eventually reached their target with only four wickets down and 7.5 overs to spare . 
1000000000000000

CRICKET - RUN-OUT GIVES LEWIS AND ENGLAND SLIM SATISFACTION . 
0000305000

LONDON 1996-08-25 
50

Chris Lewis did his best to forget his controversial omission from the England one-day squad on Sunday but could not prevent Pakistan reasserting their dominance in the final test at The Oval . 
340000000000500000000500000000560

A super piece of fielding by Lewis , dropped as a disciplinary measure after arriving only 35 minutes before the start on the fourth morning , provided the only bright spot for England as the touring team batted on to reach 413 for five at the interval , a lead of 87 . 
00000030000000000000000000000000500000000000000000000

The solitary wicket to fall was Asif Mujtaba , run out for 13 attempting a second run to third man where Lewis was lurking with a point to prove . 
000000340000000000000300000000

There seemed scant danger until the Surrey player swooped on to the ball and returned off balance to county team mate Alec Stewart who whipped off the bails . 
00000010000000000000034000000

Lewis , though , could not make similar waves with the ball as Salim Malik and Wasim Akram batted through the rest of the session with few alarms . 
30000000000003403400000000000

Wasim rattled along to 30 not out , outscoring his partner who was unbeaten on 24 at the break , although the weather was again threatening to play the dominant role . 
30000000000000000000000000000000

Rain arrived just as the players left the field for lunch , forcing the ground-staff into action yet again . 
00000000000000000000

The weather delayed the resumption for over an hour , the umpires finally announcing play would start again at 1445 local time ( 1345 GMT ) . 
000000000000000000000000700

BASEBALL - ORIOLES SNEAK PAST ANGELS . 
0010010

BALTIMORE 1996-08-25 
50

Rafael Palmeiro 's two-out single in the sixth inning scored Roberto Alomar with the go-ahead run as the Baltimore Orioles rallied past the California Angels 5-4 and took over the American League 's wild-card berth on Saturday . 
34000000003400000012000120000078000000

The Orioles trailed 4-3 when pinch-hitter Mike Devereaux led off the sixth with a triple against reliever Kyle Abbott ( 0-1 ) and scored the tying run on Alomar 's single . 
01000034000000000340000000003000

After Brady Anderson sacrificed , Palmeiro hit the first pitch into right field for a single , scoring Alomar . 
03400300000000000030

In Boston , former Mariner Darren Bragg 's first career grand slam in the sixth inning off reliever Randy Johnson lifted the Boston Red Sox to their fifth win in six games , a 9-5 victory over Seattle . 
050034400000000000340012200000000000050

" Just one of those things , I was just trying to make contact , " said Bragg . " 
00000000000000000300

The bases were loaded and I had two strikes . 
0000000000

I was just trying to put the ball in play . 
00000000000

I got the good part of the bat on it and it carried out . " 
0000000000000000

In Cleveland , Kevin Seitzer 's two-out single in the top of the 10th brought home David Hulse with the winning run as the Milwaukee Brewers sent the Cleveland Indians to their third straight extra-inning defeat 4-3 . 
01034000000000003400000012001200000000

Bob Wickman ( 5-1 ) , acquired from the New York Yankees on Friday , earned the win in his Milwaukee debut despite allowing the tying run in the eighth inning . 
34000000012200000000100000000000

At Minnesota , Marty Cordova and Matt Lawton hit solo homers and Frankie Rodriguez allowed six hits over seven innings to earn his first win as a starter in a month as the Minnesota Twins held on to beat the Texas Rangers 6-5 . 
05034034000034000000000000000000012000001200

" Yeah , you know it 's fun , it 's always fun when you 've got a chance to go to the ballpark and win a game that 's important , " said Rodriguez . " 
0000000000000000000000000000000000300

Every game should be important , but it 's a little more important now . " 
0000000000000000

In New York , Wally Whitehurst allowed two runs over seven innings for his first win in more than two years and Paul O'Neill 's three-run double snapped a sixth-inning tie as the New York Yankees held on for a 5-4 victory over the Oakland Athletics . 
05603400000000000000003400000000012200000000120

Whitehurst , promoted from Triple-A Columbus on Wednesday , allowed seven hits and struck out one without a walk . 
30001200000000000000

It was his first win since defeating the St. Louis Cardinals on May 28th , 1994 when he was with the San Diego Padres . 
0000000012200000000001220

In Kansas City , Jose Rosado came within one out of his third complete game and Michael Tucker homered and drove in three runs as the Kansas City Royals broke a six-game losing streak with a 9-2 victory over the Detroit Tigers in a battle of cellar-dwellers . 
056034000000000034000000001220000000000012000000

Rosado ( 5-3 ) allowed two runs -- one earned -- and seven hits over 8-2/3 innings with three walks and six strikeouts . 
300000000000000000000000

In his last four starts , the 21-year-old left-hander has given up only four earned runs in 29-2/3 innings .

00050000000

LISBON 1996-08-25 
50

Portuguese champions Porto kicked off the season with a disappointing 2-2 home draw against Setubal and were lucky to squeeze in an equaliser in extra time . 
701000000000001000000000000

Porto , who are fighting to take their third consecutive title this season , were 2-0 down until the 86th minute when a header by Mario Jardel found the net after a string of missed opportunities , including a penalty taken by top league scorer Domingos Oliveira in the 60th minute . 
1000000000000000000000000340000000000000000003400000

Domingos redeemed himself by netting the equaliser just into extra time . 
300000000000

Setubal , who put on a skilful counter-attack throughout the game , opened the scoring 16 minutes into the match when an unmarked Chiquinho Conde shot around Porto 's new Polish keeper Andrejez Wozniak . 
10000000000000000000000340010070340

Conde scored his second in the 70th minute . 
300000000

Benfica , also playing their first game of the season at home , were held to a 1-1 draw by northern side Braga despite the fact that the visitors were reduced to 10 men in the 54th minute after Rodrigo Carneiro was sent off for a second bookable offence . 
10000000000000000000001000000000000000034000000000

Benfica dominated the game but their lack of a first-class striker was apparent throughout and in the 30th minute they lost key Brazilian midfielder Valdo who suffered a light knee injury . 
10000000000000000000007030000000

He was substituted by Paulao . 
000030

Benfica finally opened the scoring in the 81st minute with a penalty taken by Helder after Luis Baltasar tripped up captain Joao Pinto under the referee 's nose . 
10000000000000303400034000000

Braga defender Idalecio gave his team their equaliser seven minutes from the final whistle with a header into the back of the net .

SOCCER - FIORENTINA WIN WITH BATISTUTA DOUBLE . 
00100300

MILAN 1996-08-25 
50

Argentine striker Gabriel Batistuta gave Fiorentina the perfect 70th birthday present on Sunday with two goals that gave the Italian Cup winners a 2-1 Supercup victory over serie A champions Milan . 
70340100000000000007800070078010

The victory , coming on the eve of the founding of the Florence club in 1926 , also marked the first time since the pre-season trophy between the Cup winners and league champions was started in 1988 that the Cup winners had won . 
00000000000050000000000000007000000000070000

Batistuta gave Fiorentina the lead in the 11th minute . 
3010000000

Sweden 's Stefan Schwarz picked him out with a lob to the edge of the box and Batistuta did the rest , chipping veteran defender Franco Baresi and scoring at the near post . 
5034000000000000030000000340000000

Montenegrin midfielder Dejan Savicevic equalised for the home team , weaving past a defender , checking and firing in a left-footed shot in the 21st minute that gave young Fiorentina goalkeeper Francesco Toldo little chance . 
703400000000000000000000000001034000

The scored stayed level to the final minutes but with a penalty shoot out looming , Batistuta took charge . 
00000000000000003000

French international midfielder Marcel Desailly fouled the Argentine , whose coach at Boca Juniors before he joined Fiorentina in 1991 was new Milan coach Oscar Tabarez , and Batistuta rammed home the free kick from 30 metres out . 
700340070000120001000010340030000000000

The 83rd minute shot , curling over the defence and dipping in under the bar from the striker dubbed Batigol by adoring Fiorentina fans , was just reward for Fiorentina who looked a far more impressive team . 
00000000000000000003001000000100000000

Milan 's player of the year George Weah missed a good first half opportunity but otherwise looked a little rusty while Italian team mate Roberto Baggio did not play due to injury . 
100000340000000000000700340000000

New Dutch signing Edgar Davids came on late in the second half as a Milan substitute but made little impact . 
070340000000001000000

The league season starts on September 8 . 
00000000

00300007800

50

Andrea Ferrigato of Italy sprinted to his second cycling World Cup win in successive weekends with victory in the Swiss Grand Prix on Sunday . 
3405000007800000000778000

Ferrigato , winner of the Leeds Classic last Sunday with a one second win over Britain 's Max Sciandri , posted a similarly narrow margin of victory again . 
30000780000000050340000000000

The 26-year-old Italian surged past compatriot Michele Bartoli and last year 's winner and defending World Cup champion Johan Museeuw of Belgium in the final few metres of the 237km race . 
00700034000000078034050000000000

All three clocked the same time of five hours 51 minutes , 52 seconds . 
000000000000000

Former world champion Lance Armstrong of the United States was in front as the leading pack of seven riders turned into the Oerlikon velodrome for the final one lap sprint but quickly faded and settled for fourth . 
00034005600000000000005000000000000000

The back-to-back wins vault Ferrigato from sixth to second in the overall World Cup rankings with 112 points but Museeuw continues to hold a commanding lead with 162 points after eight of the 11 rounds .

RUGBY UNION - All Blacks relive triumph . 
12012000

PRETORIA , Aug 25 - Captain Sean Fitzpatrick and his All Blacks revisited the test venue today to relive some of the magic moments of yesterday 's momentous rugby victory over South Africa , NZPA reported . 
5000003400120000000000000000000560100

Most of the test 15 who beat the Springboks 33-26 to secure New Zealand 's first-ever rugby series in South Africa stood in the middle of the empty 50,000-seat Loftus Versfeld . 
00000000100056000005600000000560

Magnificent , ' ' said Fitzpatrick , New Zealand 's most capped player and the world 's most capped forward . 
000003056000000000000

The players relived the moves and tries , the tackles and what might have been as the emotions of victory continued . 
0000000000000000000000

Zinzan Brooke , the only No 8 in test rugby to have scored a dropped goal when he kicked a three-pointer against England during last year 's World Cup , added a second to his name yesterday . 
34000000000000000000005000078000000000

I was right here , ' ' he said standing at the spot where he had received the ball for the kick . 
00000000000000000000000

The maul was there and I was going to go in but I thought I should hold off because we had the ball . 
000000000000000000000000

When ( halfback ) Justin Marshall got the ball he was going to go on the openside where Jon Preston was so I emptied my lung at him to get the ball this way . 
00003400000000000034000000000000000

I just hit through and I was punching the air before the ball got there . 
0000000000000000

It cost me a few bucks at the bar . ' 
00000000000

' 
0

The decision to attempt a dropped goal was a spontaneous one , Brooke said . 
000000000000300

It was just like the World Cup , the ball came and the chance was there . ' 
000007800000000000

' 
0

Centre Frank Bunce said he had never felt so exhausted during a match . 
03400000000000

We were gutted and there was nowhere to hide , they just kept coming at you , ' ' he said . 
0000000000000000000000

I was gone in the first 20 minutes , completely exhausted , but you had no choice . 
000000000000000000

There was just so much riding on it . 
000000000

It 's amazing just how big this ground was yesterday . ' 
000000000000

' 
0

Two-try winger Jeff Wilson said he was so tired that he kept asking Bunce where he should be while defending . 
003400000000030000000

He told me I 'm buggered too so just hang in there ' , ' ' Wilson recalled . 
0000000000000000300

About 4000 New Zealander supporters were partying into the early hours of today in the South African capital . 
0078000000000007800

Messages of goodwill continued to roll into the team hotel . 
00000000000

All Blacks coach John Hart said Prime Minister Jim Bolger rang him today to offer his congratulations . 
120340003400000000

He thanked us on behalf of the country , which is really nice for the team , and I understand we had tremendous support at home . ' 
0000000000000000000000000000

01200

South Africa yet to hear from apartheid enforcers . 
560000000

Anton Ferreira 
34

CAPE TOWN 1996-08-25 
560

South Africa 's truth commission begins issuing subpoenas this week in a bid to dig beneath the political rationales and find the sinister figures who have the blood of the country 's race war on their hands . 
56000000000000000000000000000000000000

Leaders of the major parties involved , from right-wing whites to radical blacks , appeared before Archbishop Desmond Tutu 's Truth and Reconciliation Commission last week to paint the broad picture of their actions for or against apartheid . 
000000000000000003401222000000000000000

Most , including former president F.W. de Klerk and African National Congress Deputy President Thabo Mbeki , offered apologies for any mistakes they had made and accepted broad responsibility for the actions of their foot soldiers . 
0000034401220034000000000000000000000

But none named those guilty of ordering or carrying out any of the gross violations of human rights which Tutu is investigating . 
00000000000000000003000

Human rights lawyer Brian Currin said the hearings last week were not intended as a form of confessional and that those who personally committed crimes during apartheid would testify only before a separate arm of the commission , the amnesty committee . 
000340000000000000000000000000000000000000

" I do n't think one should have expected more than what one got , " he said . " 
00000000000000000000

That was not the amnesty committee where perpetrators are expected to open their hearts and souls and to tell it all . " 
00000000000000000000000

The commission , which has the power to grant amnesty to those who confess to abuses , has begun hearing the testimony from people already in jail for their deeds . 
0000000000000000000000000000000

But others , such as self-confessed secret police hit-squad leader Dirk Coetzee , have yet to testify . 
000000000034000000

Tutu 's deputy chairman , Alex Boraine , told reporters the commission would begin issuing subpoenas to suspects who refused to appear voluntarily some time this week . 
3000034000000000000000000000

He added that former hardline apartheid president P.W. Botha could be among those called . 
000000034000000

But Currin , who is advising several people regarded as perpetrators , said this was not the best way to achieve the commission 's aims . 
03000000000000000000000000

" A person can be forced to appear , but the only way one is going to get to the truth in its totality is if people feel it is a good idea to go to the amnesty committee . 
0000000000000000000000000000000000000000

At the moment this is not the case . " 
0000000000

He cited Coetzee , who was charged with murder after confessing in media interviews to dirty tricks . 
003000000000000000

His trial is due to start in December but the truth commission intends to decide on his amnesty application before that . 
0000000000000000000000

Currin said the law had to be changed so all judicial prosecutions were automatically suspended for those who approached the truth commission . 
30000000000000000000000

Last week 's submissions to the commission by the ANC , de Klerk 's National Party and the right-wing Freedom Front of General Constand Viljoen left many South Africans unsatisfied . 
0000000001034012000120034007800

Boraine said the picture was incomplete because officers of the apartheid-era security forces had yet to make their scheduled , separate submission , but one black caller to a radio talk show declared : 
3000000000000000000000000000000000

" This whole thing is utterly useless , it does n't help us at all . 
0000000000000000

What the people expect is to have houses , to have jobs . " 
00000000000000

Political scientist Jannie Gagiano said he doubted that the National Party , which implemented apartheid in 1948 and began dismantling it in 1990 , felt it carried a burden of guilt and needed to be exculpated through the commission . 
0034000001200000000000000000000000000000

" Therefore I have some doubts about achieving some form of reconciliation . 
0000000000000

One has to feel a bit guilty to feel the need for reconciling yourself to a historical adversary , " he said . 
00000000000000000000000

Professor Tom Lodge of the University of the Witwatersrand demurred , saying : 
0340012220000

" In the irritation , in the jokes , in the anger that white South Africans express about the commission , I think there 's a moral uneasiness , and I think that 's healthy . 
000000000000007800000000000000000000

Responsibility is percolating downwards . " 
000000

Moslem refugees seek to vote in Serb-held town . 
700000700

Samir Arnaut 
34

MATUZICI , Bosnia 1996-08-25 
5050

Thousands of Moslem refugees denounced Bosnia 's elections as a farce on Sunday because Serb incomers would be able to vote in their old home town , cementing partition of the country . 
007005000000007000000000000000000

They said they were ready to force their way back across post-war ethnic lines to Serb-held Doboj , one of several towns where NATO troops fear violence involving refugees determined to vote where they once lived . 
0000000000000007500000010000000000000

The refugees , rallying in Matuzici on government territory two km from Doboj in northeast Bosnia , waved banners calling the polls a farce staged by the United Nations and the European Union . " 
00000500000050050000000000012001200

We demand to vote in Doboj , " other banners said . 
000005000000

Bosnia 's Moslem-led central government and many displaced Moslems are angered by a key provision of the Western-organised September 14 elections allowing people to vote in post-war " new places of residence . " 
5070000070000000070000000000000000

As a result , separatist Serb authorities have packed former Moslem majority towns with refugees of their own or registered other Serbs to vote there . 
00000700007000000000070000

Critics say that what was billed as an electoral process to reintegrate Bosnia as a single , multi-ethnic state is shaping up as a referendum on partition , de facto or de jure . 
0000000000005000000000000000000000

" Only our physical presence in Doboj will mean that the Dayton peace treaty has truly been implemented , " Edhem Efendija Camdzic , Doboj 's Islamic imam-in-exile , told the refugees . 
000000500005000000003440507000000

" The main point of this rally is to highlight to the world powers what misfortune they brought upon us , " said Reuf Mehemdagic , head of Doboj municipality-in-exile . 
0000000000000000000000034000500

" Eleven thousand Serbs who came from elsewhere to Doboj will vote there . 
00070000050000

How can we then expect the reintegration of Bosnia ? 
0000000050

But no one will stop us from returning to our homes . " 
0000000000000

Mirhunisa Komarica , a government refugee official , said : " We want to vote where we were thrown out from . 
3400000000000000000000

This is a protest of warning and the next step is entering our town using all means possible , so let them shoot . " 
0000000000000000000000000

Bosnian Vice President Ejup Ganic , a Moslem , told the refugees : " We have a message for the Serbs who are now in our homes not to plan the future of their children there because there will be no good fortune in that . " 
70034007000000000000700000000000000000000000000

To loud applause , he added : " We will enter Doboj , untie the Doboj knot and ensure free movement for all . 
000000000005000500000000

We have to enter Doboj to free the Serbs from their own ( separatist ) politics . " 
000050007000000000

The Dayton peace accords guaranteed refugees the right to return to their homes and ensured freedom of movement across ethnic lines . 
0500000000000000000000

But local police , controlled by nationalist parties in Moslem , Serb and Croat sectors of Bosnia , and civilian mobs have turned ceasefire lines into virtually impassable borders . 
000000000707070050000000000000

The majority of refugees from Bosnia 's 1992-95 war are Moslems from the Serb-controlled north and east . 
000005000070070000

NATO-led peace troops beefed up their presence in the Doboj area on Sunday to deter any sudden emotional attempt by the refugees to cross the Inter-Entity Boundary Line into Doboj . 
7000000005000000000000000566050

But the crowd dispersed without incident . 
0000000

Moslems and Serbs have scuffled several times along the line in the past when Moslem refugees tried to surge into the town . 
70700000000000700000000

Eight killed in Moscow casino blaze . 
0005000

MOSCOW 1996-08-25 
50

Corporate America taking new view on compensation . 
05000000

Anne Murray 
34

NEW YORK 1996-08-23 
560

Corporate America is planning major changes in employee compensation in the next few years , according to a recent study . 
050000000000000000000

What it comes down to is this : If you 're highly skilled , you 'll benefit nicely . 
0000000000000000000

But if you 're not and cannot contribute to your employer 's goals , you 'll be paid less . 
00000000000000000000

The survey , conducted in late 1995 and the early part of this year by management consulting firm Towers Perrin , showed that the focus will be on an employee 's overall value to the company 's bottom line -- rather than how well an employee performs a specific task . 
000000000000000000120000000000000000000000000000000

Presently , for example , if an accountant 's job involves doing five specific tasks , he or she can expect a certain salary , said Sandra O'Neal , a Towers Perrin principal . 
0000000000000000000000000034001200

In the future , the accountant will be evaluated solely on " knowledge , skill and abilities , " she said . 
0000000000000000000000

In addition to using accounting skills , the accountant will also have to be creative , work well in a team , be sensitive to customer needs and set productivity goals . 
00000000000000000000000000000000

" The good news is , if you 're highly skilled and have many abilities , you 'll be paid more , " said O'Neal . 
00000000000000000000000030

" The bad news is , if you 're not skilled and ca n't contribute to a team , to customer service and the organisation 's goals , you 'll be paid less . " 
00000000000000000000000000000000000

Of the 750 mid-to-large size corporations surveyed , 81 percent had undergone a major restructuring in the last three years , and more than two-thirds reported that productivity and profits were up as result . 
00000000000000000000000000000000000

Next on the agenda for these firms is developing a new compensation structure , and 78 percent report that they are considering a new , skills-based plan for both management and non-management employees . 
0000000000000000000000000000000000

This coming shift , O'Neal said , " is not just isolated or a fad . 
0000300000000000

It 's an inexorable change . " 
0000000

After World War II , corporations adopted a " military model " creating hierarchical organisations where " the concept of defined tasks worked great , " she said . 
07880000000000000000000000000

But as the economy became global , customers were more demanding and problems became more complex . 
00000000000000000

" Multi-layers kept management at a distance from its customers , " O'Neal said . 
000000000000300

Now organisations must change to stay competitive . 
00000000

O'Neal says firms will place a greater emphasis on teams and team performance in giving raises . 
30000000000000000

If your team does well , you 'll do well . 
00000000000

If it does n't do well , do n't expect a raise . 
0000000000000

Is this fair to an employee who can go the distance but is on a team that ca n't keep up ? 
0000000000000000000000

" That 's an important question we used to ask a lot , " said O'Neal . " 
000000000000000300

It 's not a question we ask any more . 
0000000000

The more important question is -- ' Do we have results ? ' 
0000000000000

" 
0

To get those results , 27 percent of the companies surveyed plan to eliminate base pay increases in favour of cash bonuses and incentives , such as employee and team award programmes and education . 
00000000000000000000000000000000000

Companies that can change their culture and view employees as business partners will do well , O'Neal said . 
0000000000000000300

For example , the survey rated some participants in the survey as " high-performing " companies , based on their return on equity above 16 percent . 
000000000000000000000000000

Those companies also said they already offer employees variable pay and business education , give their managers more control over pay decisions and celebrate employee and team success . 
00000000000000000000000000000

" They respect employees more , they trust employees more and they value their employees more , " O'Neal said . 
000000000000000000300

" The key to success at high-performance companies is engaging employees in a business partnership . 
0000000000000000

It will improve a company 's bottom line . " 
0000000000

FEATURE - Fertile Ukraine faces drought of cash and rain . 
00050000000

Irene Marushko 
34

BATKIVSHCHYNA COLLECTIVE FARM , Ukraine 1996-08-26 
566050

Four shiny new green-and-yellow John Deere combines parked at this 1,750-hectare ( 4,325-acre ) farm in the grain-growing regions south of Kiev do n't fill its chief agronomist with enthusiasm . 
0000340000000000000005000000000

" They did a good job this year , but they need good diesel and good engine oil , " said Ivan Odnosum . " 
0000000000000000000003400

God help us if there is a breakdown , " he said of the machinery , loaned to the farm after the Ukrainian government bought it earlier this year . 
300000000000000000000070000000

The country 's grain harvest this year is forecast to fall by more than 23 percent to only 28 million tonnes and two harsh factors are to blame . 
00000000000000000000000000000

A drought scoured the steppes in May and June , stunting the growing wheat . 
000000000000000

And the farming sector , making the painful transition from Soviet central planning to a market economy simply has no money . 
0000000000700000000000

Ukraine 's black soil is so fertile that a diplomat described it as " rich enough to grow rubber boots " . 
5000000000000000000000

But recently Ukraine has been losing its reputation as a breadbasket of Europe , earned in the years before brutal forced collectivisation under Soviet dictator Josef Stalin . 
0050000000005000000000070340

" The wheat will not be of a good quality this year , " said Hryhory Borsuk , a scientist at the Mironivka Wheat Institute , run by the Ukrainian Academy of Agrarian Sciences . 
00000000000000034000001220000122220

" The temperature on the ground reached 62 decrees Celsius ( 143.60 Fahrenheit ) this summer . 
00000000070000000

We 've never seen anything so bad , " he said in an interview in his office , unlit since the government cut off electricity because of unpaid power bills . 
0000000000000000000000000000000

The harvest is gathered in the dry areas , but rainfall in Western Ukraine has delayed harvesting there . 
0000000000005600000

While Mironivka 's scientists , some unpaid for months , carry on developing new strains of wheat resistant to Ukraine 's extreme continental climate , Borsuk said the lack of cash in Ukraine 's agricultural sector is as bad as the drought . 
0100000000000000000500000300000050000000000

Collective farms and Ukraine 's nascent private farming sector have no money for fertiliser , no money for herbicides and pesticides , no money to repair old or buy new machinery , no money for fuel , and none to buy good seed . 
00050000000000000000000000000000000000000000

This year 's harvest is down from last year 's 36.5 million tonne harvest , which in turn compares with 50 million tonnes in 1990 , the year before independence . 
0000000000000000000000000000000

The decline is all the worse for people who recall wasteful Soviet times , when the Kremlin imported grain but priced bread so cheaply that people bought it to feed their pigs . 
000000000007000050000000000000000

" Agriculture is very expensive , and there are no solutions to our problems on the horizon , " said Odnosum . 
0000000000000000000030

He said his farm , its 260 workers now readying the fields for winter wheat sowing , expected the land to yield 5.2 tonnes per hectare ( 2.5 acres ) but ended up with 3.9 tonnes -- still better than the national average of 2.11 tonnes per hectare this year . 
000000000000000000000000000000000000000000000000000

" We did not have money for fertiliser , we 're in debt for fuel , and we 're borrowing diesel , " Odnosum said . 
00000000000000000000000300

A few kilometres ( miles ) down the two-lane road which passes Odnosum 's farm , where the occasional horse-drawn buggy passes by , is the 1,700-hectare ( 4,200-acre ) Shevchenko collective farm , built next to a village still neat and tidy despite post-Soviet decay . 
00000000000030000000000000000030000000000000700

Chief Accountant Natalya Sypron said the collective is strapped for cash , earlier this year bartering 220 tonnes of grain for diesel to fuel six rickety grain combines and tractors badly in need of repairs and basic maintenance . 
003400000000000000000000000000000000000

The average family earns 160-200 million karbovanets a year ( $ 800 - $ 1,000 ) -- but many have not been paid in months , Soprun said . " 
000000000000000000000000003000

People are working out of their own dedication . " 
0000000000

Borsuk said the farm sector has two options : " We can sit down and cry , or we can do something . " 
300000000000000000000000

He said the government plans to increase the sowing of the winter wheat which will be harvested next year . 
00000000000000000000

Planted in late summer and early autumn , the grain is Ukraine 's largest export item and traditionally grows better than summer wheat in Ukraine 's soil . 
0000000000050000000000005000

Further plans , he said , called for full provision of resources like fertiliser and herbicides for 25 percent of Ukraine 's arable land next year , for 50 percent in 1998 and 100 percent of the land in 1999 . 
00000000000000000000500000000000000000000

" If we follow this we 'll be able to sell 10 million tonnes of grain by the year 2000 , " Borkus said . 
0000000000000000000000300

The government has been trying to phase out huge subsidies to the farm sector , and in a move back to pre-Soviet days has given up to 50 hectares ( 124 acres ) of land to some 36,000 private farmers willing to go it alone . 
0000000000000000000007000000000000000000000000

Collective farms will last for the next few years , because most private farms now only produce enough to feed themselves with maybe a little extra to sell , said one private farmer : " In the future , maybe , but it 's better not to hurry . 
0000000000000000000000000000000000000000000000000

" Collectivisation brought us a lot of pain . 
000000000

And it went too fast . 
000000

Privatising too quickly can also have a negative outcome . " 
00000000000

100000

Melanie Cheary 
34

JOHANNESBURG 1996-08-26 
50

Gencor Ltd on Monday said it had swelled its year attributable profit and streamlined operations to strengthen it for the current financial year despite a variety of divisional setbacks . 
120000000000000000000000000000

Announcing the group 's results for the year ended June 30 , chairman Brian Gilbertson said : " Happily the strong improvement in financial performance is not an illusion arising from the recent weakness of the rand relative to the dollar . " 
0000000000000340000000000000000000000000000

Gencor raised attributable earnings to 1,803 million rand from 1,003 million rand previously - in dollar terms an increase to $ 469 million from $ 279 million - and won despite the group 's Impala Platinum Holdings Ltd posting dismal results . 
100000000000000000000000000000000012220000

" Not everything has gone well . 
0000000

We 've had substantial production difficulties at a number of our operations . 
0000000000000

The most obvious one with the greatest effect on the corporation was at Impala where we had the furnace failure , " Gilbertson said . 
0000000000000100000000300

Implats posted year attributable profit of 176 million rand from 281 million previously . 
10000000000000

Not only did the company lock in 3.92 rand per dollar in February / March , but it suffered output losses due to a furnace shutdown last August . 
00000000000000000000000000000

The rand was last bid at 4.5350 against the dollar . 
00000000000

Nor was Implats the only operation to fail output targets . 
00100000000

Ingwe Coal Corporation Ltd was hit hard by heavy rains . 
12220000000

It forfeited nearly one million tonnes of production to flooding at its mines in Mpumulanga province . 
00000000000000500

But Gilbertson said the greatest gloom in the year came from the European Commission 's blocking of Implats ' proposed merger with Lonrho Plc 's platinum interests . 
0300000000001200010000120000

" The big disappointment for the year was the failure of the platinum merger . 
000000000000000

From Gencor 's perspective we are taking the position that it is not on , " Gilbertson said . 
0100000000000000300

Looking ahead to the current financial year , he said that Gencor would boost earnings further . 
00000000000100000

" Gencor is well placed to take up the challenges of the future . 
01000000000000

The group is soundly structured and prudently financed and is blessed with an excellent portfolio of world-class businesses . 
0000000000000000000

I think we can look forward to further growth " . 
00000000000

Citing the disposal of Gencor 's stake in industrial holdings group Malbak Ltd for one billion rand among other smaller disposals , Gilbertson said Gencor had pruned its portfolio to concentrate on core assets . 
00001000000120000000003010000000000

" We 've tried to clean up our overall portfolio by disposing of non-core assets . 
0000000000000000

The biggest of those was Malbak . 
0000010

Overall a very substantial pruning ... 
000000

leaving Gencor clearly structured along commodity lines , " Gilbertson said . 
010000000300

He added that the group still had about 85 million rand after tax invested in various shares , which were market for disposal when required . 
00000000000000000000000000

Referring to Gencor 's increased 41.5 percent stake in Ingwe , Gilbertson said the group would wait for coal shares to be cheaper before considering snapping up more . 
00100000010300000000000000000

" I think we would have liked to have more of Ingwe but it 's the question of adding value . 
000000000001000000000

When we bought the shares we bought ... 
00000000

at quite a bit lower than the price is now ... 
00000000000

maybe if we just wait another few years for the next downturn in coal . " 
0000000000000000

Finally , Gilbertson said a growing proportion of Gencor 's income was coming from offshore and unlisted investments .

Advanced Medical buying IVAC Medical . 
120120

SAN DIEGO 1996-08-26 
560

Advanced Medical Inc. said Monday it will buy IVAC Medical Systems Inc. , a former Eli Lilly & Co . 
12200000122200012220

unit , for about $ 400 million in cash , creating one of the world 's largest makers of intravenous infusion therapy products . 
000000000000000000000000

Under the agreement , IVAC and Advanced Medical 's wholly owned subsidiary , IMED Corp. , will merge to form a new company that will develop and manufacture infusion pumps that regulate the amount of intravenous fluid being administered to a patient , as well as proprietary disposable products . 
00001012000001200000000000000000000000000000000000

The combined company will have estimated revenues of $ 353 million . 
000000000000

Advanced Medical , through IMED , is already one of the nation 's largest developers and manufacturers of intravenous infusion pumps and proprietary disposable products . 
12001000000000000000000000

It has sales in 38 foreign countries . 
00000000

San Diego-based IVAC is a major provider of infusion systems and related technologies to the health-care industry . 
781000000000000000

It has manufacturing plants in San Diego ; Creedmoor , N.C. ; Hampshire , England ; and Tijuana , Mexico , and distributes its prodcuts in more than 120 countries . 
0000056050505050050500000000000

Eli Lilly sold IVAC on Dec. 31 , 1994 to DLJ Merchant Banking Partners LP , River Medical Inc. and other investors . 
12010000001222201220000

Advanced Medical said it expects to take an unspecified one-time charge to pay for the merger . 
12000000000000000

It did not say when the charge would be taken . 
00000000000

" The addition of IVAC is expected to contribute to financial results in the full second quarter of 1997 , " the companies said . 
0000100000000000000000000

The merger will add to both companies ' historical leadership in infusion therapy and technology-based drug delivery devices , they said . 
0000000000000000000000

In 1968 , IVAC introduced the world 's first infusion therapy monitoring device . 
00010000000000

A year later IVAC improved its system with the addition of an IV pump that regulated the flow of liquids through positive pressure . 
000100000000000000000000

IMED introduced the world 's first volumetric infusion pump in 1974 . 
100000000000

IMED had profits of $ 1.7 million , or 6 cents per fully diluted common share , on $ 53.9 million in revenues in the first half of 1996 . 
100000000000000000000000000000

Excluding the effect of a one-time restructuring charge of $ 17.4 million , IVAC had net income of $ 4.2 million on net sales of $ 112.8 million for the 1996 first half . 
0000000000000100000000000000000000

Advanced Medical reported profits of $ 8.4 million on sales of $ 29.2 million in the quarter ended June 30 . 
120000000000000000000

William J. Mercer , IVAC president and chief executive officer , will become the president and CEO of Advanced Medical . 
344010000000000000120

He led the transition of IVAC to a privately held company and was previously senior vice president at Mallinckrodt Group Inc . 
0000010000000000001220

Joseph Kuhn , Advanced Medical and IMED president , will become the new company 's executive vice president and chief financial officer . 
34012010000000000000000

The deal is expected to close by the first quarter of 1997 , subject to regulatory approval . 
000000000000000000

It has already been approved by both companies ' boards . 
00000000000

Mark Gleeson 
34

JOHANNESBURG 1996-08-26 
50

The tiny islands of the Seychelles failed to make soccer history at the weekend when they bowed out of the preliminary rounds of the African Nations Cup . 
0000050000000000000000007880

Trailing fellow Indian Ocean islanders Mauritius 1-0 from the first leg , they were held to a 1-1 draw at home on Saturday despite playing against 10 men for most of the match . 
0056050000000000000000000000000000

The 2-1 aggregate took Mauritius into the group phase of the qualifiers for the 1998 finals , and kept up the Seychelles ' record of never having won an official match in their 10 years of FIFA membership . 
000050000000000000000500000000000000100

The Seychelles must have thought they were on course for a historic breakthrough when Mauritian midfielder Andre Caboche was sent off for a crude tackle in the 19th minute . 
050000000000007034000000000000

But the visitors responded to the setback immediately -- veteran striker Ashley Mocude scoring a minute later to give them a two-goal aggregate lead . 
0000000000034000000000000

Although Danny Rose 's 50th-minute equaliser gave the Seychellois renewed hope they could not find the net again and were eliminated . 
0340000070000000000000

Mauritius now play in group seven of the qualifiers against Malawi , Mozambique and favourites Zambia . 
50000000005050050

Namibia , who drew 0-0 with Botswana in their first leg , won the second leg in Windhoek 6-0 to stretch their unbeaten run to eight matches and continue their remarkable progress on the African soccer stage . 
50000050000000000500000000000000007000

They now play in group five with Cameroon , Gabon and Kenya . 
0000000505050

German-based striker Bachirou Salou returned home to Togo to score the decisive only goal of their tie against Congo . 
00340005000000000050

Salou , who plays for MSV Duisburg in the Bundesliga , scored in the 53rd minute of Sunday 's match in Lome for a 1-0 aggregate win which takes his side into group six , where they will meet Liberia , Tanzania and Zaire . 
300001200700000000000500000000000000000505050

Ethiopia needed a penalty shoot-out in Addis Ababa to overcome Uganda after a 2-2 aggregate scoreline . 
50000056005000000

Both legs ended 1-1 before Ethiopia won the spot kick decider 4-2 . 
0000050000000

Uganda 's elimination follows their humiliating 5-1 aggregate defeat by Angola in June 's World Cup qualifying preliminaries . 
5000000000500078000

The other preliminary round second leg match , between Mauritania and Benin in Nouakchott , was postponed until Friday . 
00000000050505000000

Benin won the first leg 4-1 .

SWIMMING - POPOV IN `SERIOUS CONDITION ' AFTER STABBING . 
0030000000

MOSCOW 1996-08-26 
50

Russian double Olympic swimming champion Alexander Popov was in a serious condition on Monday after being stabbed on a Moscow street . 
7070034000000000000500

A doctor said it was too early to say whether Popov , the only man to retain the Olympic 50 and 100 metres freestyle titles , would return to top-level sport . 
00000000003000000070000000000000

" His condition is serious , " said Rimma Maslova , deputy chief doctor of Hospital No 31 in the Russian capital . " 
000000003400000566007000

But he is conscious and is talking and smiling . " 
00000000000

Maslova told Reuters she was not an expert in sports medicine , but said it was too early to judge Popov 's chances of returning to competitive swimming . 
30100000000000000000300000000

Popov , who won gold in the 50 and 100 metres freestyle at the recent Atlanta Olympics , was stabbed in the abdomen late on Saturday after an argument with a group of roadside watermelon sellers in south-west Moscow . 
3000000000000007800000000000000000000050

Maslova said the wound had affected a lung and a kidney . 
300000000000

Doctors operated on Popov , 24 , for three hours . 
00030000000

Popov told NTV television on Sunday he was in no danger and promised he would be back in the pool shortly . " 
30100000000000000000000

There 's no need to worry . 
0000000

We 're going to be walking soon -- and swimming , " he insisted cheerfully from his bed in the intensive care unit . 
000000000000000000000000

Interfax news agency said police had detained one of the attackers . 
100000000000

It said the row started when Popov and a group of his friends were returning from a party . 
0000003000000000000

Vitaly Smirnov , president of the Russian National Olympic Committee , said President Boris Yeltsin had given the swimmer Russia 's top award for his Olympic performance . " 
34000078880003400005000007000

I am not a doctor but I think he is doing all right , " said Smirnov . 
000000000000000030

Smirnov said the Olympic Committee might ask the government to take measures to protect the country 's best athletes , some of whom have already chosen to live abroad for fear of a surge in crime in post-Soviet Russia .

SOCCER - PLAYERS LEAVE MATCH EARLY TO CATCH PLANE . 
0000000000

Brian Homewood 
34

RIO DE JANEIRO 1996-08-26 
5660

Two key players left a Brazilian championship match early on Sunday because they had to catch a plane to Russia to play with the national team . 
000007000000000000050000000

Sao Paulo midfielder Andre and Santos defender Narciso were both substituted during their teams ' game , taken to Sao Paulo airport and flown to Rio de Janeiro in a private jet chartered by the Brazilian Football Confederation ( CBF ) . 
120301030000000000056000056600000007880700

At Rio , they joined up with the national team squad for the journey to Moscow , where Brazil will face Russia in a friendly international on Wednesday . 
05000000000000050050050000000

The problem arose because the Sao Paulo-Santos clash was selected as the day 's televised live match , forcing it to be put back three hours from the usual kickoff time . 
00000120000000000000000000000000

Santos suffered more from their loss as Narciso 's replacement Jean gave away a penalty from which Sao Paulo scored the decisive goal in a 2-1 win . 
1000000300300000012000000000

Sao Paulo lead the first stage of the championship on goal difference from surprise package Juventude , who beat Internacional 2-1 . 
1200000000000001000100

Corinthians , who played in a tournament in Spain last week , also faced a plane marathon as they attempted to keep up with a hectic fixture list . 
10000000500000000000000000000

They were due to leave Spain Monday night , arrive in Sao Paulo on Tuesday morning , catch another plane to the southern city of Curitiba one hour later and then play away to Atletico Paranaense in the Brazilian championship the same evening . 
00000500000560000000000005000000001200700000

Botafogo striker Tulio , who was overlooked by Zagalo for the tour which also features a game away to the Netherlands on Sunday , scored his third goal in three games as the defending champions beat Bahia 2-1 away . 
1030000030000000000050000000000000001000

Tulio , who has been top-scorer in the competition for the last two seasons , has been struggling against injury for most of this year . 
30000000000000000000000000

TENNIS - QUENCH YOUR THIRST - IF YOU CAN AFFORD IT AT U.S. OPEN . 
000000000000780

Bill Berkrot 
34

NEW YORK 1996-08-26 
560

A message on television monitors all around the National Tennis Centre reads : " Due to hot weather please seek shade and drink plenty of fluids " -- sound advice until you check out the price of fluids . 
000000005660000000000000000000000000000

Perhaps the advisory was cut off before concluding : " ...and bring plenty of money . " 
00000000000000000

A small bottle of a garishly-coloured sports drink at the sun-drenched U.S. Open is going for $ 3.75 , while a litre of basic , life-sustaining water will set you back $ 4.00 -- for water ? 
0000000000078000000000000000000000000

" At the Olympics water was only a dollar , and that was the Olympics , " said one incredulous fan , noting that the Atlanta Games had been notorious for price gouging . 
0007000000000070000000000780000000

U.S. Open officials managed to insult most of the male tennis players last week with their controversial handling of the seeding and draw . 
780000000000000000000000

When the tournament began on Monday it was the fans ' turn to be offended . 
0000000000000000

" That baked lasagna better be good for $ 8.50 , " said New Yorker Rebecca Weinstein , a U.S. Open regular who was eating a sandwich she had brought from home . 
000000000000078340078000000000000

A trio of hungry fans at the food court who had already forked over the lasagna money pronounced it good , but Carol Perry chimed in , " The water is ridiculous , they want four dollars for the water , you might as well get a glass of wine . " 
0000000000000000000000340000000000000000000000000000

Indeed , a nice glass of chardonnay or white zinfandel was going for $ 4.75 , while an imported beer was just a bit more than the water at $ 4.50 . 
00000000000000000000000000000000

What 's the message here ? " 
0000000

Maybe they want us to be alcoholics , " Perry joked before lifting her glass of wine . 
000000000300000000

Fans will be shelling out $ 12.50 for a hamburger and a large french fries . 
0000000000000000

And that little snack is guaranteed to make you thirsty . 
00000000000

Make that $ 16.50 . 
00000

Even a sandwich as pedestrian as a ham and swiss cheese is going for a whopping $ 8.00 . 
0000000000000000000

Of course , it is served on a tuscan roll . 
00000000000

It must be the cost of flying those rolls over from Tuscany every day that drives up the price of the sandwich . 
00000000000500000000000

TENNIS - HUBER AND MALEEVA FALL , UP-AND-COMERS ADVANCE AT OPEN . 
003030000070

Larry Fine 
34

NEW YORK 1996-08-26 
560

Martina Hingis led a youthful charge and Australian Open finalist Anke Huber and Magdalena Maleeva were fallen seeds on Monday in a hot , sunny opening to the U.S. Open tennis championships . 
340000078034034000000000000078000

The 15-year-old Hingis , seeded 16th , was honoured to play the first match of the season 's last Grand Slam on Stadium Court but happy to hurry off with a straight-sets victory over the 112th-ranked Angeles Montolio of Spain . 
00300000000000000007805600000000000034050

" It was very hot and I did n't want to stay long on the court , " said a cheery Hingis , who had no worries in racing to a 6-1 6-0 victory against the overmatched Spaniard . 
000000000000000000000300000000000000070

Hoping for a longer engagement on the cement at Flushing Meadows were the sixth-seeded Huber of Germany and 12th seed Maleeva of Bulgaria . 
000000000560003050003050

Huber , who lost to Monica Seles in the Australian Open final , fell victim to an unfortunate draw in bowing to dangerous floater Amanda Coetzer of South Africa . 
300003400780000000000000340560

Coetzer , ranked 17th , avenged her defeat to Huber in the Australian Open semifinals by winning 6-1 2-6 6-2 . 
300000000300780000000

" I looked at it as not a first round match , just a great challenge for me , " said Coetzer , 24 . " 
00000000000000000000030000

I was really concentrating on keeping my own momentum and my own rhythm . 
00000000000000

" She is tough to play in that way because she plays very up and down . 
00000000000000000

She played one great game and than a few errors . 
00000000000

The challenge was just for me to keep playing my own game . " 
00000000000000

Huber , who reached the final a week ago at Manhattan Beach , could only mourn her luck of the draw . 
3000000000560000000000

" I was n't happy when I saw the draw . 
00000000000

She was the first non- seeded player , " said the 21-year-old German . " 
000000000000700

It 's always tough to play somebody like that in the first round in a Grand Slam . 
000000000000000780

" I think I did n't play that bad today . 
00000000000

It was maybe my best first round match in a Grand Slam I ever played . " 
00000000007800000

Monday brought the best out in U.S. Open rookie Aleksandra Olsza of Poland , ranked 110th . 
00000078034050000

The 18-year-old Olsza , last year 's Wimbledon junior champion , celebrated her debut in the main draw of the Open by removing Maleeva 6-4 6-2 . 
003000070000000000007003000

The curtain-raising victories by Hingis and Olsza provided a ringing endorsement for the newest wave of women 's players coming up from the junior ranks . 
00003030000000000000000000

The Swiss teenager , a twice French Open junior champion and a Wimbledon juniors winner , had already proven her main stage mettle by reaching the quarters at this year 's Australian Open . 
0700007800007000000000000000000780

" I hope I can get into the last 16 , " said Hingis , seeded to face third seed Arantxa Sanchez Vicario in the fourth round . 
0000000000000300000034400000

Hingis has been working hard on conditioning and has lost eight pounds ( 3.5 kilos ) in advance of the championships . 
3000000000000000000000

" There will be tough matches but I hope I can get there , " she said . " 
0000000000000000000

Then we 'll see if Arantxa will be there , too . " 
0000030000000

The fast-moving Olsza , 18 , was cool in her opening match . 
0030000000000

" I was n't scared when I heard that I was playing Maleeva , " said Olsza . " 
0000000000003000300

I know that if I want to play professional tennis I have to do my best to try to beat her and I ca n't be scared . " 
00000000000000000000000000000

Olsza is undaunted by the level of competition in the pros . 
300000000000

" In terms of tennis , I think the junior players are really good now . 
0000000000000000

In a few years , it could change a lot among the top players . " 
0000000000000000

Two big-serving women 's players made quick work of Japanese opponents . 
000000000700

TENNIS - STICH GLAD HE STAYED AFTER OPEN VICTORY . 
0030000700

Richard Finn 
34

NEW YORK 1996-08-26 
560

Michael Stich nearly pulled out of the U.S. Open in protest over the men 's seeding fiasco but the former Wimbledon champion was glad he stayed after sweating out a four-set win on Monday over qualifier Tommy Haas . 
340000078000000000007000000000000000340

" I still feel it 's embarrassing what happened and I was about to pull out yesterday and say , ' That 's it , ' " said Stich , one of a host of men who cried foul over seeding procedures that forced an unprecedented remaking of the men 's draw last week . 
0000000000000000000000000000300000000000000000000000000

" But there are so many reasons to play , especially spectators and the kids who come out here and want to enjoy watching tennis , that I decided to stay . " 
000000000000000000000000000000000

In a break from tradition , the Open did not seed in strict accordance with ATP rankings , instead taking into account other factors that raised objections of favourtism toward U.S. players . 
000000070000000100000000000000500

One prominent player that did not stay for the Open was French Open champion Yvegeny Kafelnikov , who after being dropped three spots from his ATP ranking to a seventh seeding , withdrew and returned home to Russia . 
000000000707803400000000010000000000050

Kafelnikov had pulled out of last week 's tournament with a rib injury . 
30000000000000

At a news conference attended by approximately 50 players on Sunday , U.S. Davis Cup player Todd Martin expressed the players ' outrage at the seedings . 
000000000000578034000000000

" The way the U.S. Open has seeded here , tampering with the ranking system , has tarnished the image and reputation of this U.S. Open in the players ' mind , and we think that is damaging to our sport , " Martin said . 
0000780000000000000000007800000000000000000300

Stich said he felt the players ought to have organised an active protest . 
30000000000000

" I feel that we made it a little easy for the USTA . 
00000000000010

They did n't really get hurt as much as I think they should have , " said Stich . " 
00000000000000000300

I feel that we should have maybe just cancelled out the Monday , not show up today and start the tournament tomorrow . " 
000000000000000000000000

But once the 27-year-old Stich got on the court , he focused his energies on trying to win the year 's last Grand Slam . 
0000300000000000000000780

He took a positive first step with his 6-3 1-6 6-1 7-5 win over compatriot Haas on a sun-baked Grandstand court . 
0000000000000003000700

Others advancing early on Monday included 11th-seeded American Malivai Washington , the Wimbledon runner-up , Sweden 's Magnus Gustafsson , and two-time former French Open champion Sergi Bruguera of Spain , who will be Stich 's next opponent . 
000000073400700503400007803405000030000

The suspicion , however , lingers in Stich 's mind that U.S. Open officials did tamper with the seeding process in order to benefit homegrown players . 
000000030007800000000000000

" I get the feeling that everything is done here for the American players and they forget about all the other players , " said Stich , who lost the 1994 Open final to Andre Agassi . 
0000000000007000000000000300000700340

It was Agassi who was at the centre of the controversy that engulfed the tournament since the original draw was completed on Wednesday . 
003000000000000000000000

The flamboyant American star was bumped up two spots from his ATP ranking of eight to a seeding of six . 
007000000001000000000

" He ( Agassi ) should be seeded the way he is playing tennis right now , " said Stich about the unfairness of moving up Agassi , who made early exits from the French Open and Wimbledon . 
000300000000000000030000003000000078070

Stich , not seeded here for the first time since 1990 , might have benefitted from some fiddling with the seedings himself after Kafelnikov withdrew . 
30000000000000000000000300

Ranked 18th in the world , Stich might have been slipped into that spot ahead of Spain 's Felix Mantilla , who is 16th but had never been played in the Open and had been left out of the seedings originally . 
000000300000000050340000000000070000000000

But Stich did n't want to play that game . 
0300000000

" I think he deserves to be seeded as everybody else who is in the top 16 deserves to be seeded , " Stich said . 
00000000000000000000000300
