003000000

SAN FRANCISCO 1996-08-25

122700340000000000120000000

000000000003000000000000000000000000

It was the second-longest streak by an active player in the the majors behind Baltimore 's Cal Ripken , who appeared in his major-league record 2,282nd straight game today , a 13-0 loss to the California Angels . 
00000000000000103400000000000000000120

Bonds has been limited to a pinch-hitting role since an MRI Friday showed a mild strain of his left hamstring . 
300000000070000000000

300000001200000000000

He was back in the starting lineup Thursday night and went 1-for-2 before exiting in the third inning .

00000000000000

0000000000

The Dayton peace agreement gave the OSCE a mandate to organise Bosnian elections . 
05000010000700

01220100000000

More than 600,000 refugees have registered to vote in 55 countries around the world , representing about 20 per cent of Bosnia 's total electorate . 
00000000000000000000050000

0000000000000000010000000

000003000000000000000001000000000000

03400700010050

100000700000000000000000000

000000000000000000007000070000000000000000

After truce , Lebed faces tougher Chechen problem . 
000300700

Alastair Macdonald 
34

MOSCOW 1996-08-26 
50

Alexander Lebed may finally get to discuss his Chechen peace proposals with Boris Yeltsin on Tuesday after a lost weekend in the region when he was forced to abandon plans to sign a new political treaty with the separatist rebels . 
34000000700034000000000000000000000000000

It could be a sobering experience for the Kremlin security chief who , just two months after being appointed by the president and two heady weeks after taking charge of the Chechen crisis , had promised to wrap up the 20-month war by the weekend . 
0000000050000000000000000000000700000000000000

Despite a mood of compromise in the region after some of the worst fighting of the war , Lebed may be just finding out that concluding a long-term settlement , somewhere between rebel demands for independence and Moscow 's insistence that Chechnya remain part of Russia , will be no easy matter . 
00000000000000000030000000000000000005000500050000000

A chain-smoking former paratroop general with a sharp line in deadpan putdowns and a soldier 's knack for making life sound simple , Lebed managed to arrange an ambitious ceasefire in the region last week , days after the Russian army threatened to bomb its way back into the rebel-held Chechen capital Grozny . 
000000000000000000000003000000000000000700000000007050

He returned at the weekend , pledging to conclude a political settlement that would make this truce work where all others have failed . 
000000000000000000000000

But then he apparently thought better of it . 
000000000

Saying he needed to tidy up legal loose ends on the deal -- and also cover his back against unnamed pro-war schemers in Moscow -- he flew back to the capital empty-handed on Sunday . 
00000000000000000000000500000000000

He met Russian Prime Minister Viktor Chernomyrdin on Monday and , according to the press service of Lebed 's Security Council , could meet Yeltsin on Tuesday . 
0070034000000000030120003000

It was not clear if the start of Yeltsin 's holiday , announced later , would affect plans to talk . 
000000003000000000000

Moscow 's as yet undisclosed proposals on Chechnya 's political future have , meanwhile , been sent back to do the rounds of various government departments . 
500000050000000000000000000

It is not known what caused the delay in the peace plan . 
0000000000000

Speculation mounted last week that Lebed was operating out on a limb in Chechnya as Yeltsin , hardly seen since his reelection last month , kept out of sight and then gave an interview criticising his envoy just as he clinched a truce . 
00000300000005030000000000000000000000000000

But Chernomyrdin took pains at the weekend to insist Lebed was playing for a united team and that the proposals he took to rebel chief-of-staff Aslan Maskhadov had been agreed by Yeltsin . 
030000000300000000000000034000030

If that were the case , it was unclear why Lebed suddenly found it necessary to have the deal verified in Moscow . 
00000000003000000000050

Lebed himself said he was concerned that powerful interests in Moscow , who have profited from the war and want it to go on , would seize on any inadequacy in the deal to remove him . 
3000000000500000000000000000000000000

Maskhadov warned that Lebed risked the same fate as a former Russian army commander in the region who sought a compromise and was blown up last year by -- so the Chechens say -- Russian forces . 
3003000000070000000000000000000700700

Maskhadov may also have made new demands on Lebed , forcing him to check back with the Kremlin on what he could offer . 
300000003000000005000000

A rebel spokesman said the two military men had come close to agreement on a face-saving formula acceptable to both sides and involving a referendum on independence at some future date . 
00000000000000000000000000000000

Chernomyrdin said voters should decide Chechnya 's future but stressed there was no question of the government letting the region quit the Russian Federation -- something Moscow fears could encourage separatist tendencies in other ethnic regions , particularly in the strategic North Caucasus . 
30000500000000000000005600500000000000000560

Lebed may be be finding that closing that political gap between the two sides is more difficult than just ending a war . 
30000000000000000000000

Actor Reeve highlights Democrats ' first night . 
03070000

CHICAGO 1996-08-26 
50

The highlights of the first day of the Democratic convention on Monday were expected to feature a mix of party leaders and people who have overcome adversity . 
0000000070000000000000000000

Among the latter were gun control advocate Sarah Brady and actor Christopher Reeve and the politicians included Rep . 
0000000340034000078

Richard Gephardt and Sen . 
34000

Thomas Daschle . 
340

Here are thumbnail profiles of the convention 's key Monday speakers . 
000000000000

Sarah Brady -- The nation 's toughest gun control law is named after Ronald Reagan 's press secretary James Brady but it was his wife who was the major force behind its passage . 
3400000000000340003400000000000000

As head of Handgun Control Inc. , Sarah Brady , 54 , campaigned nonstop for tough gun control in the years following the shooting of her husband and then President Reagan in 1981 . 
0001220340000000000000000000003000

Her reward was the passage in 1993 of the " Brady Bill " which requires a mandatory five-day waiting period for purchase of handguns and also mandates background checks for would-be gun purchasers . 
0000000000780000000000000000000000

Reagan recovered fully from his wounds but Brady , who was close to death after being shot by John Hinckley Jr . 
3000000300000000003440

, suffered serious brain damage . 
000000

Sarah was Brady 's second wife and they have a son , James Scott Brady Jr . 
30300000000034440

Before the assassination attempt , she had worked for Republican congressmen and for the Republican Party . 
00000000070000120

Christopher Reeve -- Reeve was best known for playing the comic book hero Superman in four movies but his greatest heroics came in real life . 
34030000000003000000000000

Reeve , an accomplished rider who owned several horses , suffered multiple injuries including two shattered neck vertebrae when he was thrown from his horse at an equestrian event in Culpepper , Virginia , on May 27 , 1995 . 
3000000000000000000000000000005050000000

Almost entirely paralyzed , Reeve underwent extensive surgery to fuse the vertebrae to the base of the skull and prevent any further damage to his spine . 
000030000000000000000000000

That allowed him to be moved to a semi-upright position . 
00000000000

Over time he regained the power of speech , so much so that he was asked to address the opening night of the Democratic National Convention . 
000000000000000000000007880

Reeve , 43 , was classically trained as an actor but became the prototypical handsome leading man . 
300000000000000000

He performed in summer stock and soap operas before being plucked as an almost unknown to play the lead in " Superman " and three sequels . 
000000000000000000000300000

Richard Gephardt -- Gephardt , House Democratic leader , is a politician with a " Mr Clean " reputation who sought the presidency eight years ago and is widely believed to still have ambitions for the job . 
34030170000000034000000000000000000000

Gephardt , 55 , the son of a milkman from a working class district of St. Louis , is a consummate congressional insider , sufficiently skilled in compromise and the ways of the legislature to manage the often-unruly House Democrats . 
30000000000000056000000000000000000000170

A former lawyer , he was in the front line of President Bill Clinton 's battle with the Republican-led Congress over the budget but has opposed the president 's decision to sign the Republican-written welfare reform bill . 
00000000000034000071000000000000070000

He advocated tough action against foreign countries to cut U.S. trade deficits but sometimes been out of step with the party 's liberal wing . 
0000000005000000000000000

He was an opponent of abortion until 1986 and voted for President Ronald Reagan 's big tax cut bill . 
00000000000034000000

Gephardt , a red-haired square-jawed man , is a less than fiery orator . 
30000000000000

His 1988 bid for the Democratic nomination only took off after he recreated himself as a firebreathing reformer of the establishment , standing up for blue collar workers and farmers . 
0000070000000000000000000000000

Tom Daschle -- Daschle , 48 , was largely unknown outside Washington and his state of South Dakota when he surprisingly beat more prominent rivals to become Senate Democratic leader after the party lost its majority to the Republicans in 1994 . 
340300000005000056000000000170000000007000

A mild-mannered and youthful man who rose rapidly after entering the Senate in 1987 , he presented himself as a Midwest moderate , as a Democratic winner in a Republican state able to unite Senate factions . 
0000000000010000000050000700070000100

Concern that he might be steamrollered by the vastly more experienced Republican leader Bob Dole was dispelled when he showed a tough edge , outmaneuvering Dole in a wrangle over scrapping a gas tax and raising the federal minimum wage . 
00000000000703400000000003000000000000000

In his early Senate years he was seen as a " prairie populist " , working on legislation protecting farmers ' prices and also on compensating veterans sickened by Agent Orange defoliant spraying in the Vietnam War . 
00010000000000000000000000000780000780

Daschle was a key player in President Bill Clinton 's failed attempt at sweeping healthcare changes but when he became minority leader he declared he would be no water-carrier for the White House . 
3000000340000000000000000000000560

He has made clear he opposed Clinton 's signing of the Republican-initiated welfare reform bill . 
0000003000070000

He has spent his adult life in politics , coming to Congress as an aide in 1972 after three years in the Air Force and then being elected to the House of Representatives himself in 1978 .

The leading U.S. beryllium producer said in a conference call it has traditionally been pro-active regarding the workplace disease , a lung ailment which can affects a small percent of people whose immune systems are susceptible . 
0050000000000000000000000000000000000

Of the 14 remaining suits , 10 were filed by employees of industrial Brush Wellman customers and Brush Wellman liability in such suits is typically covered by insurance , Timothy Reid , vice president of corporate communications , said on the call . 
0000000000000120012000000000034000000000000

The company was responding to an article in Sunday 's New York Times . 
00000000001220

He said the article largely reiterated information about the suits and the disease which had previously been made public via Securities and Exchange Commission filings and annual reports . 
00000000000000000000122200000

" Brush Wellman has been a leader in dealing with health and safety issues ( related to chronic Beryllium disease ) for nearly 50 years , " he said . " 
0120000000000000000000000000000

We have a record of going beyond regulatory requirements ... and we consistently share the most current information available ... with customers and employees . " 
00000000000000000000000000

The customer employee suits were filed in 1990-95 , he said . 
000000000000

A class action filed by a former Brush Wellman employee in April 1996 was dismissed in July , he said . 
000000012000000000000

The company is " vigorously defending " the remaining four suits filed by former and current Brush Wellman employees , he said . 
00000000000000001200000

After a delayed opening , the stock was off 1-1/2 to 18-7/8 .

Tapie to quit French assembly seat as film opens . 
3007000000

PARIS 1996-08-26 
50

Former businessman and soccer boss Bernard Tapie said that he would give up his seat in the National Assembly by Wednesday , the day a film by Claude Lelouche in which he stars opens in France . 
0000034000000000012000000003400000050

" I will no longer be deputy by the time the film opens , " he said in a broadcast interview . 
0000000000000000000000

" Just about , " he told Europe 1 radio when asked whether he had sent his letter of resignation to Assembly speaker Philippe Seguin . 
00000001200000000000010340

A Seguin spokeswoman confirmed that no letter or call had yet been received . 
03000000000000

Tapie , 53 , was resigning just ahead of expected government action to eject him from the Assembly following a finding by the Supreme Court that he was bankrupt and thus ineligible for public office for a five-year period . 
3000000000000000010000012000000000000000

Tapie , the target of a blizzard of legal actions over his now-destroyed business empire and the Marseille soccer team he once ran , has a starring role in Lelouche 's " Homme , femmes : mode d'emploi " ( Men , women : instructions for use ) . 
3000000000000000010000000000030000000000000000000

He plays a power-hungry lawyer in the movie described as " a tender and cruel comedy " by Lelouche , who is making his 35th film . 
000000000000000000300000000

" I have paid too dearly for mixing two careers , " Tapie said . " 
0000000000003000

In France , you cannot be a film artist and a national politician at the same time . 
050000000000000000

That is why I will no longer be deputy by the time the film opens . " 
00000000000000000

Justice Minister Jacques Toubon began last month the formal process of ejecting Tapie from the French parliament as well as stripping him of his seat in the European parliament . 
003400000000300700000000000700

The French procedure was expected to be completed before October 2 , when the National Assembly is to reconvene after a summer break , but the European procedure was expected to take longer . 
0700000000000012000000000070000000

Tapie 's lawyer has said he intends to appeal to the European Court of Human Rights in an effort to prevent or delay the loss of his European seat . 
300000000001222200000000000700

But such an appeal , even if the court were to accept the case , which it is not obliged to do , would not suspend enforcement of the French judgement against him . 
0000000000000000000000000000070000

Tapie faces a probable spell in prison after he loses his parliamentary immunity , since two appeal courts have confirmed jail sentences of eight and six months against him for tax fraud and rigging a soccer match . 
30000000000000000000000000000000000000

He is appealing in both cases to the Supreme Court .

FOCUS - Eurobourses end mixed but London recovers . 
001000500

Leonard Santorelli 
34

LONDON 1996-08-27 
50

European bourses closed mixed on Tuesday with London clawing back most of the day 's losses despite an unsteady start on wall Street , hit by inflation worries . 
70000005000000000000012000000

The dollar weakened during the day with many dealers sidelined because of uncertainty over Tokyo 's monetary direction ahead of the important Japanese Tankan economic survey out on Wednesday . 
000000000000005000000071000000

But it recovered at the close of trade . 
000000000

Stocks in London started the week badly after a three-day weekend , slipping 0.3 percent , but bargain-hunters later moved in and the FTSE index recovered most of the lost ground to end only just in negative ground . 
005000000000000000000007000000000000000

Tuesday 's patchy showing in London followed a string of records last week , culminating in Friday 's trading high of 3,911 , fuelled by a wave of European interest rate cuts . 
000005000000000000000000000070000

The London bourse drew little help from the unsettled morning on Wall Street , which slipped in and out of positive ground after a stronger-than-expected August consumer confidence report refuelled inflation fears , pulling U.S. Treasuries back from their early peaks . 
050000000005600000000000000000000012000000

Shortly after the report appeared showing the confidence index rising to 109.4 in August from a revised 107.0 in July , Wall Street relinquished virtually all its morning gains . 
000000000000000000000560000000

" Treasuries remain very sensitive to any indication of a strong economy and we 're still in that summer doldrum period of light trading , " said Alan Ackerman , market strategist at Fahnestock & Co . " 
01000000000000000000000000034000012200

Consequently , stocks and bonds are both subject to rapid swings . " 
0000000000000

Frankfurt was the one bright spot in Europe . 
500000050

Floor trading ended up 0.25 percent and the computerised IBIS index climbed nearly 0.4 percent , given a push by the performance of chemical shares . " 
000000000700000000000000000

The market is trading 100 percent on fundamentals at the moment as interest rate fantasy disappears -- it 's all company news , " said one trader . 
0000000000000000000000000000

French shares ended slightly down amid growing unease about a difficult autumn for the government which also weighed on the franc , dealers said . 
7000000000000000000000000

Bond prices were weaker and the franc was quoted at 3.4210 per mark for the first time since August 13 as worries about the government 's autumn budget and a weak U.S. currency lifted the mark and squeezed French investments . 
00000000000000000000000000000005000000700

The dollar , which dropped sharply on Monday because of jitters over the Japanese Tankan survey , weakened further in quiet trading but regained losses to end the day close to Monday 's levels . 
00000000000007100000000000000000000

" Besides the Tankan , there 's nothing really until the U.S. jobs numbers next week , " said a UK bank corporate dealer . " 
00010000000500000000500000

There is still the summer malaise hanging over the market . " 
000000000000

Foreign exchange markets regard the Tankan report as an important indication of the country 's future monetary policy direction . 
00000100000000000000

If it points to weakness in the economy , the report will help the dollar regain some lost ground as speculation of a near-term rise in Japanese interest rates will evaporate . 
00000000000000000000000000700000

The Japanese discount rate is currently at a record low of 0.5 percent . 
07000000000000

The dollar was also pressured by the mark 's strength against European currencies amid renewed concerns over Europe 's economic and monetary union ( EMU ) timetable . 
0000000000070000050000007000

CURRENCIES 
0

The dollar was at 1.4788 marks and 107.74 yen at the close of European trading compared with 1.4789 marks and 107.55 yen on Monday .

" You only have to see them in action at protests , " said David Harding , spokesman at ARC , Hanson 's aggregates company . " 
000000000000003400010100000

They walk around with mobile phones and camera equipment , they communicate and gather support for demos via the Internet -- we 're talking about a highly sophisticated organisation . " 
0000000000000000000700000000000

One road protestor under the codename Steady Eddie told construction journal " Building " earlier this year , " If it comes down to full-scale economic warfare , we will aim to drive them out of business . " 
000000340000100000000000000000000000000

As well as financial threats , companies also emphasise the " terror " tactics used . 
0000000000000000

Costain 's contract to build the controversial Newbury bypass , which runs through a conservation area , has led to violent protests delaying building , bomb threats , staff intimidation and picketing of chief executive Alan Lovell 's home . 
1000000500000000000000000000000000034000

A Costain spokesman told Reuters : " We 've had all sorts of protests at the head office and the chief executive 's house . 
0100100000000000000000000

But it 's when it gets to the ( employee ) families -- that it goes across the line . " 
000000000000000000000

Tactics used by some underground groups including the cryptic Berkshire Wood Elves , which distribute leaflets with instructions on home-made explosives , are now the subject of a police investigation . 
0000000001220000000000000000000

Other larger activist groups include Earth First , The Land is Ours , Alarm UK and Road Alert . 
0000012012220120120

The groups have targeted specific projects like the Newbury bypass and the M3 motorway through Twyford Down in the southern county of Hampshire . 
000000005000500560000050

But they are also campaigning on broader issue such as stopping the government road building programme and out-of-town superstores which they say create more traffic , pollution and damage local communities . 
00000000000000000000000000000000

The government has slashed its road-building spending . 
00000000

Although protests may have contributed to the decision it has been seen primarily as economic rather than ecological . 
0000000000000000000

Graham Watts , chief executive of the Construction Industry Council , said : " I do n't think many firms involved in tendering for sensitive projects realise the impact environmental activity has on the cost of running a project . 
3400000122000000000000000000000000000000

" But they are more alert than they were 3-4 years ago . 
0000000000000

There 's no doubt it 's a big issue now . " 
000000000000

He says the damage comes in two forms : " Tangible -- in the form of extra costs , additional security , threats to staff and the more intangible damage caused by negative publicity . " 
000000000000000000000000000000000000

Watts said the cost of protesting can be heavy once the company is locked into a contract . 
300000000000000000

" I do often hear on the industry circuit of tales where the company tenders at low margins and the demonstrations which follow means they are running the project at a loss . " 
0000000000000000000000000000000000

ARC says it 's not just contractors in the front line but also suppliers like itself . 
10000000000000000

Its own quarries came under attack after it emerged that it may be a supplier for the Newbury bypass . 
00000000000000000500

" It was called the " First Battle of the Newbury bypass ' , " said ARC 's Harding . 
00000078888800001030

" We had 300 Earth First protestors invade and occupy our site . 
0000120000000

Hundreds of thousands of pounds ( dollars ) of damage was done in one day . 
0000000000000000

Plus there was the knock-on cost of lost production and extra security in future . " 
0000000000000000

Simon Brown , analyst at investement bank UBS , said this new phenomenon has led to a change in the way the industry evaluates project risk . 
340000010000000000000000000

" When talking to Tarmac about the M3 link ( through Twyford Down ) they made it fairly clear that their risk assessment methods have been changed and now involve a very clear environmental risk analysis . " 
00001005000560000000000000000000000000

Harding says others have done the same . " 
300000000

As a result of eco-terrorism we are looking at controversial jobs more closely to see if the profit margins are wide enough to cover things like extra security . " 
000000000000000000000000000000

For an industry already suffering from razor-thin margins , overcapacity and stagnant demand , eco-terrorism is the latest bizarre twist in the construction sector 's tale of woe . 
00000000000000000000000000000

London Carnival ends in high spirits . 
7800000

LONDON 1996-08-26 
50

London 's annual Notting Hill Carnival , the largest in Europe and second in the world only to Rio , ended peacefully on Monday with an estimated 800,000 revellers singing and dancing the day away in high spirits . 
500788000050000000500000000000000000000

Police said they made 30 arrests and there were two stabbings . 
000000000000

But there was no repeat of the ugly scenes that used to scar the street festival , and police praised the crowds over the two days of festivities as good-natured . 
0000000000000000000000000000000

Around 400 police were wounded in riots in 1976 when the carnival , now in its 31st year , acquired its darker reputation from which it is now only slowly recovering . 
00000000000000000000000000000000

Shopkeepers still board up their windows and many residents leave town for the weekend , but for four or five years there has been no disorder and relatively little crime . 
0000000000000000000000000000000

340340000344000000078800000000000

The Spaniard has not played for nearly a year because of rheumatoid arthritis in both his feet , and organisers of a pairs event to be staged in Bordeaux , France from October 17 to 20 have been asked to provide him with a buggy .

000070000000000000000003030007800

0003000000000

0030000000000000000000000

0000000000000000000

TENNIS - EDBERG EXTENDS GRAND SLAM RUN , TOPPLES WIMBLEDON CHAMP . 
003000000500

Larry Fine 
34

NEW YORK 1996-08-27 
560

Stefan Edberg produced some of his vintage best on Tuesday to extend his grand run at the Grand Slams by toppling Wimbledon champion Richard Krajicek in straight sets at the U.S. Open . 
340000000000000007800703400000780

Edberg , competing in the 54th consecutive and final Grand Slam event of his illustrious career , turned back the clock at Stadium Court with a flowing 6-3 6-3 6-3 serve-and-volley victory over the fifth-seeded Dutchman . 
3000000007800000000000560000000000070

" It 's a win that I can be proud of , " said the 30-year-old Swede , winner of two U.S. Opens and six Grand Slam titles in all . " 
00000000000000007000050007800000

It 's never easy to beat the Wimbledon champion . " 
00000007000

Edberg , who has said he will retire at season 's end , made it look easy under gray skies at the National Tennis Centre . 
30000000000000000000005660

The unseeded Swede struck quickly , breaking Krajicek in the first game and never let loose his grip on the one hour 44 minute match as he served and volleyed with the grace that made him one of the dominant players of his time . 
007000030000000000000000000000000000000000000

" There 's not doubt about it , Richard was definitely off his game and I took advantage , " said Edberg . 
00000000300000000000030

" I still have my days where I feel great out there . " 
00000000000000

Also reaching the second round were top-seeded defending champion Pete Sampras , a 6-2 6-2 6-1 winner over last minute replacement Jimy Szymanski of Venezuela , called on after Adrian Voinea of Romania withdrew because of a sprained ankle . 
0000000003400000000003405000034050000000

Third seed Thomas Muster of Austria also charged into the second round with a 6-1 7-6 ( 7-2 ) 6-2 romp over Javier Frana of Argentina . 
003405000000000000000034050

Marcelo Rios of Chile , the 10th seed , also advanced . 
340500000000

30000000050340

BASEBALL - GIANTS EDGE PHILLIES 1-0 . 
0010100

SAN FRANCISCO 1996-08-27 
560

William VanLandingham pitched eight scoreless innings and Glenallen Hill drove in the game 's only run with a first-inning single as the San Francisco Giants claimed a 1-0 victory over the Philadelphia Phillies on Monday . 
340000034000000000000012200000012000

VanLandingham ( 8-13 ) , who entered the game with one complete game in the first 56 starts of his career , limited the Phillies to two hits and two walks with four strikeouts . 
30000000000000000000000010000000000

" We 've been working all year on my follow-through , and I really concentrated on that , " VanLandingham said . " 
00000000000000000003000

It gave me more life in all of my pitches , so the ball moved more . " 
000000000000000000

At Colorado , Andres Galarraga homered and drove in three runs as the Colorado Rockies had 10 extra-base hits and Billy Swift won his first game in almost a year in a 9-5 rain-shortened seven-inning victory over the Cincinnati Reds . 
05034000000001200000340000000000000000120

Swift ( 1-0 ) , who made his first start since June 3rd and underwent arthroscopic surgery on his right shoulder earlier in the season , allowed five runs and six hits in five innings . 
300000000000000000000000000000000000

In Houston , Andy Benes allowed two runs over seven innings and Royce Clayton had a run-scoring single in the seventh to lift the St. Louis Cardinals to a 3-2 victory over the Houston Astros . 
050340000000340000000000122000000120

Benes ( 14-9 ) allowed five hits , walked five and struck out 10 for his 11th win in 12 decisions . 
3000000000000000000000

The Cardinals moved within one-half game of first-place Houston in the National League Central Division .

BASEBALL - ORIOLES WIN , YANKEES LOSE . 
00100100

BALTIMORE 1996-08-27 
50

Cal Ripken 's bases-loaded walk scored Brady Anderson with the winning run in the bottom of the 10th as the Baltimore Orioles regained control of the top spot in the wild-card race with a wild 12-11 victory over the Oakland Athletics . 
340000340000000000001200000000000000000120

Trailing by a run entering the 11th , the Orioles rallied against Oakland reliever Mark Acre ( 0-2 ) with a walk and a triple by Brady Anderson to tie the game . 
000000000100103400000000003400000

Then Oakland manager Art Howe decided to intentionally walk Rafael Palmeiro and Bobby Bonilla to load the bases but Acre was nowhere near the plate to Ripken . 
0103400003403400000300000030

The decisive pitch nearly hit Ripken and gave the Orioles a one-half game lead over the Chicago White Sox in the wild-card race . 
000003000100000012200000

In Seattle , Jay Buhner 's eighth-inning single snapped a tie as the Seattle Mariners edged the New York Yankees 2-1 in the opener of a three-game series . 
05034000000001200122000000000

New York starter Jimmy Key left the game in the first inning after Seattle shortstop Alex Rodriguez lined a shot off his left elbow . 
1203400000000103400000000

The Yankees have lost 12 of their last 19 games and their lead in the AL East over Baltimore fell to five games . 
010000000000000770100000

At California , Tim Wakefield pitched a six-hitter for his third complete game of the season and Mo Vaughn and Troy O'Leary hit solo home runs in the second inning as the surging Boston Red Sox won their third straight 4-1 over the California Angels . 
0503400000000000034034000000000001220000000120

Boston has won seven of eight and is 20-6 since August 2nd . 
1000000000000

The Red Sox are two games over .500 for the first time this season . 
012000000000000

In Chicago , Cal Eldred pitched 5-1/3 scoreless innings and John Jaha scored one run and doubled in another as the Milwaukee Brewers held off the slumping Chicago White Sox , 3-2 . 
050340000034000000000120000122000

Eldred ( 6-5 ) walked one and struck out three . 
00000000000

Angel Miranda retired one batter and Bob Wickman retired the next four but loaded the bases in the eighth . 
34000034000000000000

In Detroit , Jim Thome 's solo homer in the ninth inning snapped a tie and Charles Nagy pitched a three-hitter for his first win in over a month , leading the Cleveland Indians to their 11th straight victory over the Detroit Tigers , 2-1 . 
0503400000000000340000000000000012000000012000

With the score tied 1-1 in the ninth , Thome hit a 2-2 pitch from starter Felipe Lira ( 6-11 ) over the left-field fence for his 29th homer . 
000000000000000034000000000000

In Toronto , Juan Guzman allowed three runs over seven innings to make homers by Joe Carter and Carlos Delgado stand up as the surging Toronto Blue Jays held off the Minnesota Twins , 5-3 . 
050340000000000340340000012200012000

Toronto returned home from a 10-game road trip and won for the eighth time in nine games as Guzman ( 11-8 ) allowed nine hits and struck out eight without a walk .

TENNIS - CHANG , WASHINGTON ADVANCE , TWO WOMEN 'S SEEDS FALL . 
0030500000000

Larry Fine 
34

NEW YORK 1996-08-26 
560

Michael Chang is playing in his 10th U.S. Open and enjoying his highest seeding ever , but the 24-year-old American had to overcome a case of the jitters Monday before winning his first-round match on opening day . 
34000007800000000007000000000000000000

Chang , seeded second behind defending champion Pete Sampras , took two hours 40 minutes to defeat 186th-ranked Jaime Oncins of Brazil 3-6 6-1 6-0 7-6 , 8-6 in the tiebreaker . 
30000003400000000034050000000000

" I was pretty tight the whole match , " conceded Chang , one of the hottest players on tour this summer with a 16-2 record on hardcourts that included two titles and a runner-up finish . 
0000000000030000000000000000000000000

" Everyone has moments when they get tight . 
000000000

Hopefully , this will have been my nerves for the whole tournament . " 
00000000000000

Joining Chang into the second round was Wimbledon runner-up MaliVai Washington , the 11th seed , who also needed four sets to get past talented Moroccan Karim Alami 6-4 2-6 7-6 ( 7-5 ) 6-1 . 
030000070340000000000000073400000000

Washington 's win was not comfortable , either . 
300000000

The 27-year-old American hurried off the Stadium Court for treatment of an upset stomach after his two and a half hour struggle against Alami . 
0070005600000000000000030

" Towards the end of my match my stomach felt like week-old sushi , " said Washington . " 
0000000000000000500

Maybe it was a combination of the heat and something I ate . " 
00000000000000

Chang and Washington were the only men 's seeds in action on a day that saw two seeded women 's players fall . 
30300000000000000000000

Australian Open runner-up Anke Huber of Germany , the sixth seed , was undone by an unlucky draw that put her against 17th ranked South African Amanda Coetzer in her opening match . 
780340500000000000000000783400000

Coetzer claimed revenge for the semifinal defeat she suffered to Huber in Melbourne by taking a 6-1 2-6 6-2 victory . 
300000000030500000000

Last year 's Wimbledon junior champion , Aleksandra Olsza of Poland , removed another seed from the draw by eliminating number 12 Magdalena Maleeva of Bulgaria 6-4 6-2 . 
00070003405000000000003405000

Other men 's winners included a pair of former Grand Slam tournament champions whose victories set up a showdown in the second round . 
000000000780000000000000

Germany 's Michael Stich , the 1991 Wimbledon champion , and two-time French Open winner Sergi Bruguera of Spain will face each other next after beating German Tommy Haas 6-3 1-6 6-1 7-5 , and Belgian Kris Goossens 6-2 6-0 7-6 ( 7-1 ) , respectively . 
50340007000078034050000000734000000734000000000

Alex O'Brien , who scored his first professional title eight days ago in New Haven , advanced to the second round with a 6-4 1-6 6-4 6-3 win over Ecuador 's Nicolas Lapentti . 
3400000000000560000000000000050340

Wimbledon bad boy Jeff Tarango caught a break Monday when he advanced after the retirement of German Alex Radulescu due to heat exhaustion . 
700340000000000073400000

Tarango was leading 6-7 ( 5-7 ) 6-4 6-1 3-1 . 
30000000000

Chang blamed breezy conditions for some of the erratic play in his match with Oncins , who had beaten him in the round of 32 at the 1992 Barcelona Olympics . 
3000000000000030000000000000570

Chang committed an untidy 53 unforced errors , though he made seven fewer than the Brazilian , who also walloped a woeful 24 double faults . 
30000000000000070000000000

The most deflating double fault came when Oncins was serving to force a fifth set , leading 6-4 in the tiebreaker . 
0000000300000000000000

The set point came after confusion at the net on the point previous , which was awarded to Oncins after the two exchanged shots at close quarters at the net . 
0000000000000000003000000000000

First Chang approached the umpire , then Oncins , then Chang again before play finally resumed . 
03000003003000000

" Those little seconds were like an hour to me , " said Oncins , who promptly fired two serves barely contained by the baseline as he frittered away his best chance . 
000000000000030000000000000000000

Chang ran off the next three points to close out the match but for Oncins , the contest was a personal victory . 
30000000000000300000000

The 26-year-old Brazilian had risen into the top 30 in 1992 . 
007000000000

The next year a close friend was struck by a stray bullet while riding home in a car from a soccer game in Sao Paulo . 
00000000000000000000000560

He died slumped against Oncins , who subsequently lost interest in tennis . 
0000300000000

" Two months ago I started talking about quitting , " said Oncins , who decided to give it one last try and made it through the Open qualifying tournament last weekend . 
000000000000300000000000000700000

" I believe in my game again , " he said . 
000000000000

At the end of the day , a spate of withdrawals from the tournament were announced . 
00000000000000000

Eighth seed Jim Courier withdrew because of a bruised right knee , and 1988 Open champion Mats Wilander bowed out due to a groin pull , organisers said . 
00340000000000703400000000000

Women 's ninth seed Mary Joe Fernandez pulled out because of tendinitis in her right wrist . 
00003440000000000

SOCCER - MARSEILLE HOLD AUXERRE TO GOALLESS DRAW . 
001010000

PARIS 1996-08-27 
50

Former European champions Marseille held French champions Auxerre to a goalless draw in a lacklustre league match on Tuesday . 
07010701000000000000

The bill looked promising but both sides , struggling to find their form early in the season , were disappointing . 
000000000000000000000

Auxerre , who start their European Cup campaign next week against Ajax Amsterdam , dominated the match but were unable to score . 
10000780000120000000000

Unbeaten in four matches , they still trail leaders Lens by one point . 
00000000010000

Lens , who have won all their three league matches so far , host Montpellier on Wednesday night . 
1000000000000010000

Despite another dismal performance , especially in defence , Marseille restored some pride by keeping the reigning champions at bay after losing 2-1 at home to Metz last Saturday . 
000000000100000000000000001000

After two seasons in the second division and after taking on half a dozen new recruits this season , some of whom do not speak a word of French , Marseille are not playing with any fluidity . 
00000000000000000000000000007010000000

But German international goalkeeper Andreas Koepke again proved a sound investment when under pressure from the Auxerre strikers , saving his team with a number of fine parries . 
07003400000000001000000000000

Marseille now lie seventh in the league on five points .

SOCCER - NEUCHATEL TO APPEAL AGAINST CYPRIEN 'S NINE-MONTH BAN . 
00100030000

GENEVA 1996-08-27 
50

Swiss league leaders Neuchatel Xamax said on Tuesday they would appeal against a nine-month ban imposed on French international defender Jean-Pierre Cyprien for his part in a post-match brawl . 
700120000000000007003400000000

Cyprien , also fined 10,000 Swiss francs ( $ 8,400 ) , traded punches with St Gallen 's Brazilian player Claudio Moura after a match on Saturday . 
3000070000000001207034000000

When officials and coaching staff tried to intervene , Cyprien launched a flying kick at Moura , but only succeeded in kneeing St Gallen coach Roger Hegi in the stomach . 
0000000003000003000000120340000

Moura , who appeared to have elbowed Cyprien in the final minutes of the 3-0 win by Neuchatel , was suspended for seven matches and fined 1,000 francs ( $ 840 ) by the Swiss league disciplinary committee . 
300000030000000001000000000000000070000

Club president Gilbert Facchinetti said he was astonished the committee had arrived at its decision so quickly and vowed the club would appeal . 
003400000000000000000000

Neuchatel coach Gilbert Gress described the incident as " shocking " , but said Moura was also to blame . 
10340000000000300000

" Moura physically and verbally provoked Cyprien during the match . 
03000030000

The referee could not have seen it or he would have punished him , " Gress said . 
000000000000000300

" During the scuffle , Moura threw the first punch . 
00000300000

Tomorrow , if someone punches me , I would not know how to react . " 
0000000000000000

Cyprien , who won his one French cap against Italy in February 1994 , cannot play in Switzerland or elsewhere until May next year . 
3000007005000000050000000

CYCLING - BUGNO CLEARED OF DOPING . 
0030000

MILAN 1996-08-27 
50

Veteran Italian Gianni Bugno has been cleared of doping after testing positive for high levels of testosterone during the Tour of Switzerland in June , the Italian cycling federation said on Tuesday . 
073400000000000000078800007000000

" He has been cleared . 
000000

The case is closed , " a spokesman said . 
0000000000

Bugno tested positive for the banned hormone after the fifth stage of the Tour , in which he finished third overall . 
3000000000000700000000

But the spokesman said subsequent tests in Cologne proved his body produced higher-than-average testosterone levels naturally . 
00000005000000000

Bugno , who won the Giro d'Italia in 1990 and two successive world titles , was banned for three months in 1994 after testing positive for the stimulant caffeine . 
300007800000000000000000000000

Expectations that Cofinec S.A. , the Hungarian bourse 's first foreign listing , will report a disappointing first half have depressed the stock below its issue price , but analysts expect a rebound in the long term . 
00120070000000000000000000000000000000

" The first half of the year is unlikely to be as strong as expected so the company will probably be unable to reach its annual plan in 1996 , " said Gabor Sitanyi , a London-based analyst for ING Barings . 
000000000000000000000000000000003400000120

The French-registered packaging materials company , which floated its shares in Hungary in July , for most of the past two weeks hovered below the 6,425 forints / Global Depositary Receipts price of its initial offering , which was oversubscribed . 
07000000000500000000000000000000000000000

000000000000000000000000000000

" Cofinec 's first-half figures will be ... 
01000000

between one-third of two-fifths of its annual plan , " said Tamas Erdei , a Budapest-based analyst for ABN-AMRO Hoare Govett . 
0000000000034007001220

Analysts blame , at least partly , Hungary 's macroeconomic environment for the weaker figures for Cofinec which , operating in Hungary , Poland and the Czech Republic , now generates about 55 to 60 percent of its annual sales from Hungary . 
0000000500000000100005050056000000000000050

01000000000000000000005000000000000030000000010000

050000005000000000000000070000

03400012222220100000000000007000000

0000000000000000000000030

He said no exact date had been set but it was possible the local elections would take place in the spring of 1997 . 
000000000000000000000000

According to OSCE officials , Serb authorities have pressed their refugees to register to vote in towns now under Serb control , but which used to have Moslem majorities . 
001007000000000000070000000700

000000507800000000000007000000000005000

Diplomats say the effect of the electoral engineering would be to establish political control over districts they conquered and ethnically cleansed in war .

The response of the Bosnian Serbs to the OSCE 's announcement was not immediately clear . 
0000780010000000

But Bosnian Serb leaders have hinted they would boycott the poll if the municipal elections were postponed , or go ahead with their own .

Russian and rebel military commanders finally met in Chechnya on Tuesday for delayed talks aimed at finalising a ceasefire arranged last week by President Boris Yeltsin 's envoy Alexander Lebed . 
7000000050000000000000003400340

The Russian army commander in the region , General Vyacheslav Tikhomirov , arrived at the rebel-held village of Novye Atagi , some 20 km ( 12 miles ) south of the Chechen capital Grozny for discussions with rebel chief-of-staff Aslan Maskhadov . 
070000000340000000560000000000070500000340

But Lebed himself , the Kremlin security chief , is still waiting back in Moscow to meet Yeltsin over his plans for a lasting political settlement in Chechnya . 
03000500000000500300000000050

Itar-Tass news agency quoted the Kremlin press service as saying Yeltsin , who left for a state holiday home near Moscow on Monday , would hold no working meetings on Tuesday . 
10000500003000000000500000000000

Lebed interrupted talks with Chechnya 's separatists on a political deal on Sunday , saying he had to consult with Yeltsin . 
3000500000000000000030

After a meeting failed to materialise on Monday , Lebed 's spokesman said he might meet the president on Tuesday . 
000000000300000000000

But Yeltsin 's spokesman rebuffed the suggestion , saying the president had left Moscow for a holiday near the capital . 
030000000000050000000

The Russians postponed the talks after a Chechen band disarmed a column of interior ministry troops on Sunday . 
0700000700000120000

The Chechens said a renegade group seized the weapons and said on Monday they had all been returned . 
0700000000000000000

The Russian command insisted that not all the weapons were the same as those taken . 
0700000000000000

Tass said the weapons and the practical implementation of the ceasefire signed by Lebed and Maskhadov last Thursday would be on the agenda of today 's talks . 
1000000000000303000000000000

Neither spoke to reporters before the meeting , which started around 10.45 a.m. ( 0645 GMT ) . 
000000000000000700

Also in Novye Atagi on Tuesday morning , was Tim Guldimann , the Swiss diplomat who heads the Chechnya mission of the Organisation for Security and Cooperation in Europe ( OSCE ) . 
005600000340070000500012222220100

Guldimann , who helped broker an earlier truce in May , was not taking part in the Tikhomirov-Maskhadov talks . 
30000000000000000700

Lebed 's peace mission this month has stopped some of the worst fighting of the 20-month-old conflict . 
300000000000000000

Three Russian servicemen were wounded in a total of six shooting incidents overnight , Itar-Tass news agency quoted the Russian military as saying on Tuesday morning .

100000000000000007000000005000

000001000000000003000000000000000

Yeltsin 's spokesman said he might meet officials during his break , but indicated Lebed was low on the list by saying Yeltsin would need time to study the proposals before talking to him . 
30000000000000300000003000000000000

Russian news agencies also quoted the Kremlin spokesman as saying that Lebed 's representatives had not sought a meeting , hinting at an attempt by the president to put his popular and outspoken protege in his place with a lesson on protocol . 
7000005000030000000000000000000000000000000

Yeltsin , 65 , has kept a low profile since he was reelected in July , prompting new speculation that the two heart attacks he suffered last year and a rumoured drinking problem could be taking their toll , weakening his grip on affairs of state . 
30000000000000000000000000000000000000000000000

Aides have dismissed such speculation , insisting that he simply needs a rest after his energetic election campaign . 
0000000000000000000

Some analysts say the Kremlin leader , whose order sending troops and tanks into Chechnya in 1994 started Russia 's ill-fated military campaign , could merely be reluctant to put his name to a peace process which might fall apart . 
00005000000000500050000000000000000000000

But Lebed , who has no real power without his boss and has hinted at dark forces in Moscow working against him , appears to think a deal will not stick without strong backing from Yeltsin . 
0300000000000000005000000000000000030

His proposals have not been spelled out but are expected to involve a compromise between the separatists ' demand for independence and Moscow 's insistence that Chechnya remain part of the Russian Federation .

Estonian MPS see little hope of electing president . 
700000000

Belinda Goldsmith 
34

TALLINN 1996-08-27 
50

Estonia 's parliament failed for a second time to elect a president on Tuesday , dealing a blow to incumbent Lennart Meri and pushing the country towards stalemate in its choice of a new head of state . 
50000000000000000000340000000000000000

Neither Meri , who oversaw Estonia 's first steps into statehood after the collapse of the Soviet Union , nor his arch-rival , former communist Arnold Ruutel , have secured the 68 votes necessary from the 101-member parliament . 
030005000000000056000000034000000000000

Meri garnered 49 votes and Meri 34 in Tuesday 's ballot for the five-year presidency of Estonia . 
300003000000000050

A third and final vote was due to be held when parliament reconvened on Tuesday but legislators were not expecting a clear result . 
000000000000000000000000

If there is no result the decision will be ceded to an electoral college . 
000000000000000

" The votes are a strong message to Meri that he is not favoured by some politicians any more , " Reform Party head Heiki Kranich told Reuters . 
00000000300000000000012034010

Under a constitution agreed in 1992 , a year after independence , the president has no executive powers . 
0000000000000000000

His only political role is to smoothe the functioning of government in periods of crisis . 
0000000000000000

But Meri , 67 , has been accused in parliament of taking too much power and not always consulting parliamentarians before making decisions . 
030000000000000000000000

His relations with a leftist-led government have sometimes been tense . 
00000000000

His support in the first round of voting on Monday was much lower than expected , scoring only 45 votes , which political analysts put down as a vote of no confidence in his performance . 
000000000000000000000000000000000000

This support only inched up to 49 in the second vote . 
000000000000

Support for Ruutel , 68 , remained constant at 34 votes . 
003000000000

If the third vote fails to give either Meri or Ruutel 68 votes , the parliamentary speaker will convene an electoral college of 101 MPs and 273 local goverment representatives to hold a new poll that could include new nominations . 
00000000303000000000000000000000000000000

This would be the first time that the former Soviet republic has had to call together an electoral college . 
00000000070000000000

In its first presidential election in 1992 Meri won the necessary votes in in a parliamentary election against Ruutel . 
00000003000000000030

Parliamentary organisers said the exact timetable remained unclear but it would probably take about a month to organise an electoral college which could also hold several rounds of voting before a clear winner emerges . 
00000000000000000000000000000000000

But Meri 's support was not enough for the 68 needed for election and a third secret ballot will take place later in the day ( 1300 GMT ) , parliamentary officials said . 
0300000000000000000000000007000000

To win a clear mandate for the five-year presidential term , a candidate must secure 68 votes from the 101-member parliament . 
0000000000000000000000

Enn Markvart , Chairman of the National Election Commission , said 96 members of parliament voted in the second round , with 12 abstentions and one ballot paper invalid . 
340000122000000000000000000000

On Monday , in the first round of voting , Meri secured 45 votes and Ruutel 34 . 
000000000030000300

Meri 's popularity has suffered in recent years , with politicians criticising him for taking too much power and acting without consulting parliament . 
300000000000000000000000

If a third round of voting fails to give either candidate 68 votes , the parliamentary speaker has to convene an electoral college of all 101 MPs and 273 local government representatives for a new vote that could take up to a month .

Former Argentine benevolent dictator Alejandro Lanusse dies . 
07003400

BUENOS AIRES 1996-08-26 
560

Alejandro Lanusse , the former dictator who ruled Argentina for two years , died at age 78 on Monday . 
34000000500000000000

Lanusse died after being brought to a hospital a week ago following a fall at home that resulted in a blood clot in the brain . 
30000000000000000000000000

He was operated on earlier in the week but failed to recover from surgery . 
000000000000000

The former dictator , who ruled from 1971 to 1973 , was best known for allowing Juan Domingo Peron , Argentina 's famed populist leader , to return to Argentina after 17 years of forced exile . 
0000000000000000344050000000050000000

Lanusse took over the leadership of the country after five years of dictatorship . 
30000000000000

But unlike his two predecessors , Juan Carlos Ongania and Marcelo Levingston , who ruled Argentina with an iron hand , Lanusse steered the country toward democracy . 
0000003400340005000003000000

That resulted in general elections in March 1973 when the Peronists led by Hector Campora and Vicente Solano Lima returned to power . 
00000000001003403440000

Lanusse was a candidate in the election but failed to defeat his old adversories and never returned to public office . 
300000000000000000000

He was imprisoned for four years in 1951 for taking part in a coup attempt to overthrow Peron led by General Benjamin Menendez . 
000000000000000003000340

Lanusse 's rule saw the gradual rise of left-wing activism which culminated in another period of brutal Argentine dictatorship from 1976 to 1983 , during which the military launched its " dirty war " that resulted in 10,000 missing people . 
30000000000000000700000000000000000000000

In his autobiography published in 1990 , Lanusse described himself as a military man with " democratic ideas . " 
00000003000000000000

He was born in Buenos Aires in 1918 and married Ileana Bell with whom he had nine children . 
0000560000340000000

He entered the Military College in 1935 .

500000000000000500000000000000000

" Although the final draft of the treaty probably did n't totally satisfy any country , it was in general balanced , " the official People 's Daily newspaper said in a commentary . 
0000000000000000000000000122000000

India blocked the Comprehensive Test Ban Treaty ( CTBT ) at the Conference on Disarmament in Geneva , saying the pact did not contain a clause committing the five declared nuclear powers to a timetable for nuclear disarmament . 
500788807000788050000000000000000000000

New Delhi 's stance , which was seen as effectively thwarting 2-1/2 years of negotiations at the Conference on Disarmament , drew widespread but generally muted foreign criticism . 
56000000000000000788000000000

India has also pledged to oppose any forwarding of the draft treaty to the United Nations General Assembly . 
5000000000000012220

China said many countries had compromised to complete the treaty and that the issue of a disarmament schedule could be discussed in future negotiations . 
5000000000000000000000000

" The completion of the test ban treaty would be an important and practical step in the gradual process of achieving total nuclear disarmament , " it said . 
00000000000000000000000000000

China has pledged support for the pact since reaching a deal with the United States that made international inspections of nuclear sites more difficult than in earlier drafts of the accord . 
50000000000005600000000000000000

The newspaper said China advocated the complete ban and destruction of nuclear weapons but that there was little hope other nuclear powers would soon adopt the same stance . 
00050000000000000000000000000

" Some nuclear powers stubbornly uphold policies of nuclear deterrence based on first use of nuclear weapons , " it said . 
0000000000000000000000

China held on July 29 what it said would be its last nuclear test before a self-imposed moratorium that took effect the following day . 
5000000000000000000000000

China was the last declared nuclear power to announce a halt to testing .

The food poisoning epidemic caused by the O-157 colon bacillus in Sakai appears to be " settling down " , Health Minister Naoto Kan was quoted by a government spokesman as telling the cabinet . 
00000007000500000000003400000000000

The O-157 colon bacillus has been found responsible for a widespread food poisoning epidemic that has killed 11 people and made over 9,500 ill this year . 
070000000000000000000000000

Sakai , near the regional commercial centre of Osaka , has been hit hardest by the deadly bacteria , with nearly 6,500 , mostly schoolchildren , affected by the disease . 
5000000050000000000000000000000

Two children in Sakai have died from complications associated with the bacteria . 
0005000000000

Kan told a cabinet meeting on Tuesday that no new victims have been reported since August 8 , indicating that the peak has passed , at least for Sakai . 
300000000000000000000000000050

Sakai officials agreed with the assessment , but said it was too early to feel relieved . 
50000000000000000

" There are still patients hospitalised and problems which must be dealt with , " a city spokesman said , citing the issue of whether to allow children infected with the bacteria but not showing symptoms to attend school from September . 
000000000000000000000000000000000000000000

Health authorities believe school lunches were the source of the food poisoning in Sakai , but researchers have been unable to pinpoint the exact source of the infection . 
00000000000005000000000000000

The outbreak has prompted authorities to tighten sanitary standards at slaughterhouses and meatpacking plants and sparked calls for an overhaul of the nation 's school lunch programme .

0000000000000000000000000000

Japan 's Agriculture Ministry also announced that it will compile hygiene guidelines based on U.S. government methods of checking the safety of farm produce to prevent another outbreak of the epidemic . 
50120000000000500000000000000000

As of Monday , 31 children were still hospitalised in Sakai city , of whom six were in serious condition .

In April , China quashed a draft resolution by the U.N. Human Rights Commission expressing concern over continuing reports of Beijing 's violations of fundamental freedoms . 
000500000012220000005000000

After the defeat of the resolution , drafted by the European Union and the United States , China 's Foreign Ministry thanked 26 countries for backing its motion for " no action " on the document . 
0000000000120056050120000000000000000

It was the sixth year in a row that China avoided censure at the U.N. 's main human rights forum . 
000000000500001000000

China has been accused of a wide range of human rights abuses , often in violation of its own legal code , in an effort to silence dissent . 
50000000000000000000000000000

A Xinhua commentary earlier this year said a plot by the West to force its human rights standards and values on other countries was doomed to failure . 
0100000000070000000000000000

Palestinians to strike over Jerusalem demolition .

Palestinian leaders in Jerusalem called on Tuesday for a two-hour strike to protest what they called Israel 's war on Arab East Jerusalem after police demolished a building there . 
700500000000000050005660000000

7000000000000050560000000001220000000

00000000000560000000000000

Bystanders at the scene said work had begun on the building in 1991 and it had yet to be completed when the Israeli police bulldozed it . 
000000000000000000000070000

The Palestinian Authority was set up under the 1993 PLO-Israel interim peace deal . 
01200000070000

" There has been a call for a general strike between one ( 1000 GMT ) and three o'clock , " Palestinian lawmaker Ahmed Hashem Zighayer told Reuters . 
00000000000000700000070344010

" This is a war that has been declared on us and we want our people to come and see the site where they declared the war . " 
00000000000000000000000000000

Prime Minister Benjamin Netanyahu 's government , which took office in June , has said it will not allow the Authority , set up under a 1993 interim peace deal to control parts of the Gaza Strip and West Bank , to operate in Jerusalem . 
0034000000000000000010000000000000056056000050

Israel 's previous government held the same position but in general turned a blind eye to Palestinian Authority activity in the city . 
50000000000000001200000

Tuesday 's demolition came a day after PLO officials said they had bowed to Netanyahu 's demand they close offices in Jerusalem . 
00000001000000300000050

00000005000000

30000000000000001220100

505660005600000

It says it will never cede any part of the city .

70560000000

SEC adopts rules to improve investor access to best stock prices . 
100000000000

WASHINGTON 1996-08-28 
50

The Securities and Exchange Commission Wednesday approved rules designed to give stock market investors a better chance at getting the best price available for their orders . 
012220000000000000000000000

The so-called order handling rules , which were proposed last September , were approved in a 4-0 vote . 
0000000000000000000

The new rules will require specialists at stock exchanges and market makers on Nasdaq to allow customers to view price quotes from other electronic trading systems that may not be readily available to them . 
00000000000007000000000000000000000

The rules will also require that customer limit orders be displayed with prices better than those available in quotes publicly available at the time . 
0000000000000000000000000

Specialists and market makers are companies or individuals recognised as qualified to maintain an orderly market in a stock . 
00000000000000000000

In a limit order , investors specify the price at which they are willing to buy or sell , as opposed to a market order executed at prevailing prices . 
000000000000000000000000000000

" These rules are intended to empower all investors , by allowing their orders to compete on a level playing field , and by providing the disclosure they need to make informed decisions , " said SEC Chairman Arthur Levitt . 
00000000000000000000000000000000000010340

The SEC 's goal , he added , was to create " one system where one price could be available to everybody . " 
010000000000000000000000

The director of the SEC 's division of market regulation , Richard Lindsey , said Wall Street firms will probably need to spend about $ 7 million to carry out the improvements called for by the new rules . 
000010000003400560000000000000000000000

In proposing the rules last year , the SEC noted that while technology has improved , commonplace practices still existed that worked against investors ' best interests . 
0000000010000000000000000000

It noted that customers whose orders were not displayed lost the chance of getting the best possible price available in the market . 
00000000000000000000000

It also cited the potential problem of a two-tiered market in which market makers quote one price to public investors while quoting better prices in private systems , thus robbing investors without access to " hidden " quotes the benefit of the best available prices . 
0000000000000000000000000000000000000000000000

Earlier this month , the SEC settled charges of alleged malpractices on Nasdaq when the parent of the Nasdaq market , the National Association of Securities Dealers , agreed to spend $ 100 million over five years to upgrade its oversight of brokers ' trading practices . 
00000100000070000070001222200000000000000000000

The SEC dropped a third proposal that would have allowed investors with market orders to trade at a better price if there were shifts in prices before their orders were executed . 
01000000000000000000000000000000

The agency said it would monitor effects of the two new rules before considering the " price improvement " proposal again . 
0000000000000000000000

The agency also proposed rule changes that would require continuous " bid " and " ask " quotations from exchange specialists and market makers who trade more than 1 percent of a stock during any quarter on Nasdaq . 
000000000000000000000000000000000000070

The SEC 's limit order display rule will mean a major change for Nasdaq , where such orders have never been displayed . 
01000000000007000000000

The president of the Nasdaq , Alfred Berkeley , was to hold a news conference Wednesday afternoon to elaborate on the new rules ' effects on the market , the second largest in the world . 
000070340000000000000000000000000000

Passengers injured in train collision in Linz . 
00000050

LINZ , Austria 1996-08-28

A passenger train collided with a locomotive at a main railway station in Linz on Wednesday and police said around 10 people were injured . 
0000000000000500000000000

Austrian television reported earlier that more than 20 had been hurt in the accident at the station in Linz , 300 km ( 180 miles ) west of Vienna . 
700000000000000000500000000050

" One locomotive was stationary and the passenger train collided into the back of it , " a police spokesman in Linz told Reuters by telephone . 
000000000000000000000501000

The express passenger train travelling from Steyr , southeast of Linz , with around 80 people on board , hit the back of a service locomotive used to shunt wagons into sidings . 
000000500050000000000000000000000

The police spokesman said he was not sure whether any more passengers were still trapped in the wreckage . 
0000000000000000000

Doctors and medical staff from a hospital across the road from the station were at the scene of the accident within minutes and were able to treat the injured quickly , he added . 
0000000000000000000000000000000000

Greater damage was averted as the driver of the passenger train had time to apply his emergency brakes before the collision occurred , a state railways spokesman told Austrian news agency APA .

Saskatchewan Wheat Pool eyes hog market . 
1220000

WINNIPEG 1996-08-28 
50

Canada 's largest grain handling firm said Wednesday it expects to forge a partnership with hog farmers by 1997 with a view to expanding the company 's scope into pork production . 
50000000000000000000000000000000

" Saskatchewan is well positioned to take advantage of growing world markets for pork , " Saskatchewan Wheat Pool chief executive Don Loewen said in a company statement . 
05000000000000001220034000000

SWP said it was analyzing potential partnerships with hog farmers and expected the first deal to be in place in 1997 . 
1000000000000000000000

The end of Canada 's rail freight subsidy last year caused a shift in feed grain production to the eastern Prairie . 
0005000000000000000000

Analysts said livestock production would likely shift to the eastern Prairie rather than feed grains being shipped to the western Prairie . 
0000000000000000000000

SWP said it may develop pork production systems that provide farmers with large integrated units , and it may consider contracting programs between producers and packers which would operate within the existing hog market framework . 
100000000000000000000000000000000000

Saskatchewan Pork International Marketing Group has an export monopoly but some Saskatchewan farmers earlier this month called for an open market in hogs .

30000000000000000000070340505000

30000000000000

0000000000000000000003000

I do n't know if I can go any faster . 
00000000000

Who knows what will happen in the later stages ? "
